### [32] [DiG-Plan: Mitigating Early Commitment for Tool-Graph Planning via Diffusion Guidance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05728v1)
*Yansi Li,Zhuosheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 扩散引导工具图规划，可迁移至coding agent工具选择与规划

TL;DR: 提出DiG-Plan框架，通过扩散提议器生成工具集和AR精炼器预测依赖，解决了AR解码早期承诺问题，在TaskBench和API-Bank上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准AR解码存在早期承诺问题，导致组合探索不足；受掩码去噪提升覆盖率观察的启发。

Method: DiG-Plan解耦组合探索和结构精炼，采用扩散提议器生成多样工具集，然后AR精炼器进行依赖预测。

Result: 在TaskBench上相对AR基线提升10%，在复杂组合任务上提升最大；API-Bank验证跨领域有效性。

Conclusion: 提议-精炼-选择设计有效，代码已开源。

中文摘要：生成可执行工具计划需要从工具库中选择合适的子集，这是一个组合搜索问题，解空间呈指数级增长。然而，我们发现了主流方法中的一个关键错位：标准自回归（AR）解码存在早期承诺问题，即初始令牌选择严格约束了搜索轨迹。一项对照研究表明，在相同计算量下，掩码去噪将Pass@10解决方案覆盖率从AR采样的0.320提高到0.943。受此启发，我们提出了DiG-Plan框架，它将组合探索与结构精化解耦。DiG-Plan采用基于扩散的提议器通过迭代精炼生成多样化的工具集，然后使用AR精炼器进行依赖关系预测。在TaskBench上，DiG-Plan相比AR基线有10%的相对提升，在复杂组合任务上提升最大；API-Bank的结果表明，提议-精炼-选择的设计在不同领域间仍然有效。代码见https://github.com/puddingyeah/DiG-Plan。

Original abstract: Generating executable tool plans requires selecting appropriate subsets from tool libraries, a combinatorial search problem with an exponentially large solution space. However, we identify a critical misalignment in predominant approaches: standard autoregressive (AR) decoding suffers from early commitment, where initial token choices rigidly constrain the search trajectory. A controlled study shows that masked denoising raises Pass@10 solution coverage from 0.320 to 0.943 over AR sampling under matched compute. Motivated by this, we propose DiG-Plan, a framework that decouples combinatorial exploration from structural refinement. DiG-Plan employs a diffusion-based proposer to generate diverse tool sets via iterative refinement, followed by an AR refiner for dependency prediction. On TaskBench, DiG-Plan improves over AR baselines by a 10% relative margin, with the largest gains on complex compositional tasks; API-Bank results show that the propose-refine-select design remains effective across domains. Code is available at https://github.com/puddingyeah/DiG-Plan.

### [33] [SubtleMemory: A Benchmark for Fine-Grained Relational Memory Discrimination in Long-Horizon AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05761v2)
*Wenxuan Wang,Haoyu Sun,Fukuan Hou,Mingyang Song,Weinan Zhang,Yu Cheng,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长程agent记忆判别benchmark，直接关联agent评测与记忆机制

TL;DR: SubtleMemory基准测试AI助手在细粒度关系记忆区分上的能力，发现现有系统表现较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长期记忆基准很少测试代理如何保持和利用记忆关系，因此需要新基准。

Method: 构建关系控制的语义伪影，嵌入用户-代理历史，评估代理恢复关系结构的能力。

Result: 当前系统在细粒度关系记忆区分上较弱。

Conclusion: 揭示了能力缺陷，并提出了诊断协议。

中文摘要：持久的AI助手，例如OpenClaw，会在长期交互中积累大量相关的记忆。随着这些记忆的增长，它们可能相互加强、在不同上下文中产生分歧或直接冲突，使得正确的协助依赖于记忆关系而非孤立的回忆。现有的长期记忆基准很少测试代理如何在后续任务中保持和利用这些关系。为了填补这一空白，我们引入了SubtleMemory，这是一个针对长期运行AI代理中细粒度关系记忆区分的基准。SubtleMemory构建了关系控制的潜在语义伪影，其变体实例化互补、微妙或矛盾的关系，并将它们嵌入到真实的用户-代理历史中，要求代理在后续查询和指令中恢复分布式的关联结构。该基准包含1522个评估实例，跨越10个长历史，基于1090个关系控制的记忆变体集，并涵盖用户相关和非用户相关查询。评估了六个独立的记忆系统、两个带有原生记忆模块的Claw风格代理以及三个带有插件记忆模块的Claw风格代理，我们发现当前系统在细粒度关系记忆区分上仍然薄弱。我们进一步引入了诊断协议，揭示了在记忆保持、检索和下游推理阶段的不同能力谱。

Original abstract: Persistent AI assistants, such as OpenClaw, accumulate large collections of related memories over long-term interactions. As these memories grow, they may reinforce one another, diverge across contexts, or directly conflict, making correct assistance depend on memory relations rather than isolated recall. Existing long-term memory benchmarks rarely probe how agents preserve and utilize such relations during downstream tasks. To address this gap, we introduce SubtleMemory, a benchmark for fine-grained relational memory discrimination in long-running AI agents. SubtleMemory constructs relation-controlled latent semantic artifacts whose variants instantiate complementary, nuanced, or contradictory relations, and embeds them into realistic user-agent histories, requiring agents to recover distributed relational structures during later queries and instructions. The benchmark contains 1,522 evaluation instances over 10 long histories, grounded in 1,090 relation-controlled memory-variant sets and spanning user-related and non-user-related queries. Evaluating six standalone memory systems, two Claw-style agents with native memory modules, and three Claw-style agents with plugin memory modules, we find that current systems remain weak on fine-grained relational memory discrimination. We further introduce diagnostic protocols that reveal distinct capability profiles across memory preservation, retrieval, and downstream reasoning stages.

### [34] [TAPO: Tool-Aware Policy Optimization via Credit Transfer for Multimodal Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05784v1)
*Chengqi Dong,Chuhuai Yue,Hang He,yandong liu,Fenghe Tang,S Kevin Zhou,Xiaohan Wang,Jiajun Chai,Guojun Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: TAPO策略优化解决工具使用中的信用分配问题，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出TAPO方法解决GRPO在工具增强多模态搜索中的信用错误分配问题，通过反事实见证和置信门控修正，无需额外开销，提升多种RL算法性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO在工具增强搜索代理中因均匀广播轨迹级优势导致信用错误分配，浪费训练信号，该问题普遍且可纠正。

Method: TAPO利用工具参数确定性构建反事实见证，通过置信门控保守优势修正补偿错误分配的负信用。

Result: 超过一半的失败轨迹和动作存在可纠正信用错误分配；TAPO在多个基准上对GRPO、GSPO、SAPO实现一致提升。

Conclusion: TAPO是一种轻量、即插即用的方法，有效利用浪费的训练信号，提升工具增强多模态搜索代理的强化学习性能。

中文摘要：我们识别并正式表征了信用错误分配（credit misassignment）作为GRPO在工具增强的多模态搜索代理中的系统性失败模式：其将轨迹级优势均匀广播给所有令牌，导致失败轨迹中有价值的工具使用步骤与无价值的步骤受到同样的惩罚。我们进一步通过实验量化了这一现象的规模。超过一半的失败轨迹和失败的工具使用动作表现出可纠正的信用错误分配，表明浪费的训练信号既可观又在结构上可利用。基于这一见解，我们提出了工具感知策略优化（TAPO），它利用了信息采集工具的参数确定性特性：相似的调用参数定义了等价的信息采集动作，因此应共享相当的信用。TAPO在当前训练批次内构建反事实见证，并通过置信门控保守优势修正来补偿错误分配的负信用。它不需要额外的标注、模型或采样，且引入可忽略的计算开销。在多个多模态搜索基准上，TAPO对三种主流强化学习算法（GRPO、GSPO和SAPO）的强基线实现了一致的、即插即用的改进。我们的代码和模型将在录用后公开。

Original abstract: We identify and formally characterize credit misassignment as a systematic failure mode of GRPO in tool-augmented multimodal search agents: its uniform broadcast of trajectory-level advantages to all tokens causes valuable tool-use steps in failing trajectories to be penalized no differently from valueless ones. We further empirically quantify the scale of this phenomenon. Over half of failing trajectories and failing tool-use actions exhibit correctable credit misassignment, demonstrating that the wasted training signal is both substantial and structurally exploitable. Building on this insight, we propose Tool-Aware Policy Optimization (TAPO), which exploits the parameter-determinism property of information-acquisition tools: similar call parameters define equivalent information-acquisition actions and should therefore share comparable action credit. TAPO constructs counterfactual witnesses within the current training batch and compensates misassigned negative credit via confidence-gated conservative advantage correction. It requires no additional annotation, models, or sampling, and introduces negligible computational overhead. Across multiple multimodal search benchmarks, TAPO delivers consistent, plug-and-play improvements over strong baselines for three mainstream RL algorithms (GRPO, GSPO, and SAPO). Our code and models will be publicly released upon acceptance.

</details>


### [35] [Can LLMs Write Correct TLA+ Specifications? Evaluating Natural-Language-to-TLA+ Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05792v1)
*Arslan Bisharat,Brian Ortiz,Eric Spencer,Khushboo Bhadauria,TaiNing Wang,George K. Thiruvathukal,Konstantin Laufer,Mohammed Abuhamad*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次系统评估LLMs生成TLA+规范的能力，发现语义正确率仅8.6%，模型大小不是关键，提示策略和推理对齐更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TLA+在工业验证中重要但编写困难，LLMs有潜力但缺乏系统评估其是否能生成语义正确的规范。

Method: 评估30个LLM（25个开放权重+5个专有），使用205个TLA+规范数据集，对开放模型采用四种提示策略（2600次运行），专有模型用少样本提示（130次运行），通过SANY和TLC验证。

Result: 句法正确率26.6%，语义正确率8.6%，成功仅限渐进提示；模型大小不预测质量，如DeepSeek r1:8b优于70B；代码模型表现差；识别出五类幻觉。

Conclusion: 当前LLMs无法可靠生成TLA+规范，需专家监督；发布的数据集和框架支持未来研究。

中文摘要：TLA+已在亚马逊和微软等公司的工业验证中得到支持，但从自然语言编写正确的TLA+规范仍需时间和专业知识，这限制了其采用。LLMs展现出潜力，但尚无先前研究衡量它们是否能够从自然语言生成语义正确的TLA+规范。本文首次系统性地评估了基于LLM的从自然语言合成TLA+规范的方法。我们的研究评估了来自8个家族的30个LLM，使用了一个包含205个TLA+规范的精选数据集：针对25个开放权重模型采用四种提示策略（2600次运行），以及5个专有模型采用少样本提示（130次运行），所有结果均通过SANY解析器和TLC模型检查器验证。LLMs的句法正确率最高达26.6%，但语义正确率仅为8.6%，且成功案例仅限于渐进式提示。结果表明模型大小并不能预测质量，例如DeepSeek r1:8b在所有策略上均优于其70B变体，这表明推理对齐对于形式语言的重要性。代码专业化模型由于主流语言训练的负迁移而持续表现不佳。我们识别出五类反复出现的幻觉，均可追溯到特定的训练数据偏差。这些结果表明，当前的LLMs在没有专家监督的情况下无法生成可靠的TLA+规范。我们发布了评估框架、代码和数据集，以支持可重复性和未来研究。

Original abstract: TLA+ has supported industrial verification at companies such as Amazon and Microsoft, yet writing correct TLA+ specifications from natural language still requires time and expertise, which limits adoption. LLMs show promise, but no prior study measures whether they produce semantically correct TLA+ specifications from natural language. This paper presents the first systematic evaluation of LLM-based TLA+ specification synthesis from natural language. Our study evaluates 30 LLMs across eight families on a curated dataset of 205 TLA+ specifications: 25 open-weight models across four prompting strategies (2,600 runs) and 5 proprietary models under few-shot prompting (130 runs), all validated by the SANY parser and TLC model checker. LLMs achieve up to 26.6% syntactic correctness but only 8.6% semantic correctness, with successes exclusive to progressive prompting. Results show that model size does not predict quality, e.g., DeepSeek r1:8b outperforms its 70B variant across all strategies, which suggests the importance of reasoning alignment for formal languages. Code-specialized models consistently underperform due to negative transfer from mainstream language training. We identify five recurring hallucination categories, all traceable to specific training data biases. These results suggest that current LLMs do not generate reliable TLA+ specifications without expert oversight. We release the evaluation framework, code, and dataset to support reproducibility and future research.

</details>


### [36] [From Risk Classification to Action Plan Remediation: A Guardrail Feedback Driven Framework for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05805v1)
*Yuhao Sun,Jiacheng Zhang,Shaanan Cohney,Zhexin Zhang,Feng Liu,Xingliang Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 护栏反馈引导agent规划，提升安全性与实用性，含闭环反馈机制

TL;DR: TRIAD是一个集成护栏的智能体框架，通过微调语言模型输出三种决策（继续、拒绝、更新）并提供结构化反馈，指导智能体修订计划以保留良性部分，在ASB和AgentHarm上平均攻击成功率降至10.42%，实现最佳安全-实用性权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有护栏通常将整个任务统一标记为不安全，牺牲了良性部分，且缺乏对护栏干预是否导致更安全下游行为的评估。

Method: 提出TRIAD框架，微调语言模型输出继续、拒绝或更新决策及结构化反馈，将反馈注入智能体上下文形成闭环，指导计划修订。

Result: 在ASB和AgentHarm上平均攻击成功率降至10.42%，在集成护栏的基线中实现最佳安全-实用性权衡。

Conclusion: TRIAD通过迭代反馈有效平衡安全与实用性，为智能体安全提供新方法。

中文摘要：基于LLM的护栏通常通过在执行前评估提议的动作或输入来保护智能体，产生安全信号，如二元允许/拒绝决策、风险类别和/或关于潜在政策违规的解释性理由。然而，智能体的风险往往源于当原本良性的任务被不受信任的外部内容、不安全的指令或有风险的工具使用所污染时。现有的护栏通常将整个任务统一标记为不安全，从而阻止威胁但牺牲了良性部分。此外，现有工作大多孤立地评估护栏，不清楚它们的干预是否会导致更安全的智能体下游行为。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了TRIAD（Tripartite Response for Iterative Agent Guardrailing），一个集成护栏的智能体框架，利用护栏生成的言语反馈作为引导信号，使智能体在每个规划步骤中保持与良性目标一致。我们在自建训练数据集上微调语言模型，输出三种决策之一：继续、拒绝或更新，以及结构化的自然语言反馈。更新不仅允许或阻止执行，还指导智能体修改计划、避免有害组件并尽可能保留良性任务。TRIAD将此反馈注入智能体的上下文，实现后续计划修订，并在护栏反馈与智能体规划之间形成闭环。在ASB和AgentHarm上的大量实验表明，TRIAD将平均攻击成功率降低到10.42%，同时在集成护栏的基线中实现了最佳的安全-实用性权衡。我们的代码可在https://github.com/YUHAOSUNABC/TRIAD获取。

Original abstract: LLM-based guardrails typically safeguard agents by evaluating proposed actions or inputs before execution, producing safety signals such as binary allow/deny decisions, risk categories, and/or explanatory rationales about potential policy violations. However, agent risks often arise when otherwise benign tasks are contaminated by untrusted external content, unsafe instructions, or risky tool use. Existing guardrails often flag the entire task uniformly as unsafe, thereby blocking the threat but sacrificing the benign part. Moreover, existing work largely evaluates guardrails in isolation, leaving unclear whether their interventions lead to safer downstream agent behavior. To address this, we introduce TRIAD (Tripartite Response for Iterative Agent Guardrailing), a guardrail-integrated agent framework that leverages guardrail-generated verbal feedback as a guiding signal to keep the agent aligned with benign objectives at each planning step. We finetune a language model on a self-curated training dataset to output one of three decisions: proceed, refuse, or update, together with structured natural-language feedback. Rather than merely allowing or blocking execution, update guides the agent to revise its plan, avoid harmful components, and preserve the benign task where possible. TRIAD injects this feedback into the agent's context, enabling subsequent plan revision and forming a closed loop between guardrail feedback and agent planning. Extensive experiments on ASB and AgentHarm show that TRIAD reduces the average attack success rate to 10.42%, while achieving the best safety-utility trade-off among guardrail-integrated baselines. Our code is available at: https://github.com/YUHAOSUNABC/TRIAD.

### [37] [When Tools Fail: Benchmarking Dynamic Replanning and Anomaly Recovery in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05806v1)
*Dongsheng Zhu,Xuchen Ma,Yucheng Shen,Xiang Li,Yukun Zhao,Shuaiqiang Wang,Lingyong Yan,Dawei Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 工具故障下动态重规划基准，直接相关LLM agent鲁棒性

TL;DR: 提出ToolMaze基准测试，通过动态路径和错误恢复评估LLM工具集成推理，发现隐式扰动和复杂拓扑严重降低性能，且容错性提升远慢于任务执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准忽略现实工具故障，仅评估理想情况，无法衡量LLM在动态环境中的重新规划能力。

Method: 设计ToolMaze，包含DAG拓扑复杂度和2×2扰动分类（显式/隐式、临时/永久），评估扰动恢复率和试错循环。

Result: 扰动使性能普遍下降，隐式语义失败下PRR下降约37%，复杂拓扑导致无效试错；容错性随规模提升速度比任务执行慢3.66倍。

Conclusion: 动态重新规划是模型缩放或提示无法解决的独立瓶颈，需专门针对容错性和重规划能力进行改进。

中文摘要：现有的基准测试在评估LLM中的工具集成推理（TIR）时，只考虑理想的“快乐路径”，在很大程度上忽略了现实世界中的工具故障。我们引入了ToolMaze，一个用于TIR代理中动态路径发现和错误恢复的基准测试。为了将系统性的重新规划与盲目的试错区分开来，ToolMaze采用了二维设计：基于DAG的拓扑复杂度和一个2×2的工具扰动分类（显式/隐式，临时/永久）。评估表明，扰动几乎在所有模型上都会降低性能，在隐式语义失败下下降最为显著。由于系统性地过度信任损坏的输出，扰动恢复率（PRR）在这些场景中下降了约37%，而复杂的拓扑结构使代理陷入徒劳的试错循环。关键在于，代理容错性随模型规模提升的速度比基本任务执行慢3.66倍，突显了动态重新规划是一个独特的瓶颈，无法通过模型缩放或提示来解决。数据和代码可在https://github.com/Zhudongsheng75/ToolMaze获取。

Original abstract: Existing benchmarks evaluate Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) in LLMs on idealized ''happy paths'', largely overlooking real-world tool failures. We introduce ToolMaze, a benchmark for dynamic path discovery and error recovery in TIR agents. To separate systematic replanning from blind trial-and-error, ToolMaze adopts a two-dimensional design: DAG-based topological complexity and a $2 \times 2$ taxonomy of tool perturbations (explicit/implicit, transient/permanent). Evaluations show that perturbations degrade performance across nearly all models, with the sharpest drops under implicit semantic failures. Driven by systemic over-trust in corrupted outputs, Perturbation Recovery Rate (PRR) plummets by around 37\% in these scenarios, while complex topologies trap agents in futile trial-and-error loops. Crucially, agentic fault-tolerance improves with model scale $3.66\times$ slower than basic task execution, highlighting dynamic replanning as a distinct bottleneck unaddressed by model scaling or prompting. Data and code are available at https://github.com/Zhudongsheng75/ToolMaze.

Original abstract: As Large Language Model (LLM) capabilities advance, locally deployed personal agents relying on API-based remote models and external skills have emerged as a novel paradigm. This paper explores the implementation of such a harness through a novel architecture that strictly decouples statistical preference learning from semantic intent parsing. Specifically, we leverage localized statistical results to influence and modulate the selection decisions of the remote LLM. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that our decoupled approach achieves the lowest cumulative regret and highest test accuracy, significantly outperforming traditional memory-augmented agents.

Original abstract: Text-guided molecular generation with LLMs often yields invalid SMILES. This perspective reveals the limitations of existing correction strategies. Post-hoc repair can recover validity while distorting key structures, LLM-only correction can introduce unintended global drift, and generic agentic correction remains constrained by greedy single-candidate trajectories even when equipped with executable RDKit edit tools. To address these limitations, we propose AMREC, which couples molecule-aware mismatch tracking with expanded candidate exploration and trajectory-level selection. ### [41] [Retry Policy Gradients in Continuous Action Spaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05888v1)
*Soichiro Nishimori,Paavo Parmas*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 重试策略梯度方法，可启发agent探索与pass@k优化

TL;DR: 本文通过引入路径导数估计器将ReMax扩展到连续动作空间，并研究了其学习动态：ReMax能通过重塑梯度（方向与幅度）促进随机探索，且Adam可缓解梯度抑制。实验证明ReMAC算法性能与SAC相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Retry-based目标（如ReMax）从离散动作空间扩展到连续动作空间，并理解其学习动态，以探索无需显式探索奖励的强化学习算法。

Method: 引入路径导数估计器（pathwise derivative estimator）用于重试目标，提出ReMAC算法作为离线策略的Actor-Critic算法，优化ReMax目标。

Result: ReMAC无需熵正则化即可促进更高的策略熵，并在连续控制任务上达到与SAC相当的性能。此外，Adam的自适应归一化可缓解梯度阻尼。

Conclusion: ReMax方法可有效促进随机探索，其梯度重塑效应（方向偏向高熵、幅度阻尼）可通过Adam缓解，从而在连续动作空间中实现高效学习。

中文摘要：诸如pass@K和max@K等基于重试的目标优化从多个采样轨迹中获得的最佳回报，近期研究表明，这些目标无需显式探索奖励即可促进探索。在离散动作空间中，ReMax通过适应回报不确定性实现这一点。在本工作中，我们为重试目标引入了路径导数估计器，并将其用于将ReMax扩展到连续动作空间。我们研究了由此产生的学习动态，并表明，即使奖励是确定性的，ReMax也能通过重塑策略梯度景观来鼓励随机探索。具体而言，它既改变了梯度的方向，使更新偏向更高的策略熵，也改变了梯度的幅度，抑制梯度并减慢收敛。我们进一步表明，Adam的自适应归一化可以缓解这种抑制，具体取决于其数值稳定参数。在实验上，我们将该目标实例化为ReMax Actor-Critic (ReMAC)，一种使用路径导数估计器优化ReMax目标的价值-策略梯度算法。我们的实验表明，ReMAC无需熵正则化即可促进更高的策略熵，并达到与SAC相当的性能。

Original abstract: Retry-based objectives such as pass@K and max@K optimize the best return obtained from multiple sampled trajectories, and recent work has shown that they can promote exploration without explicit exploration bonuses. In discrete action spaces, ReMax was shown to do so by adapting to return uncertainty. In this work, we introduce pathwise derivative estimators for retry objectives and use them to extend ReMax to continuous action spaces. We study the resulting learning dynamics and show that, even with deterministic rewards, ReMax can encourage stochastic exploration by reshaping the policy-gradient landscape. In particular, it alters gradients both in direction, biasing updates toward higher policy entropy, and in magnitude, damping gradients and slowing convergence. We further show that Adam's adaptive normalization can mitigate this damping, depending on its numerical stabilization parameter. Empirically, we instantiate this objective as ReMax Actor-Critic (ReMAC), an off-policy actor--critic algorithm that optimizes the ReMax objective using a pathwise derivative estimator. Our experiments show that ReMAC can promote higher policy entropy without entropy regularization and achieves performance comparable to SAC.

</details>


### [42] [Evolving Agents in the Dark: Retrospective Harness Optimization via Self-Preference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05922v2)
*Wenbo Pan,Shujie Liu,Chin-Yew Lin,Jingying Zeng,Xianfeng Tang,Xiangyang Zhou,Yan Lu,Xiaohua Jia*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接优化agent harness的自监督方法，在SWE-Bench上提升，高度相关

TL;DR: 提出自监督方法RHO，仅用过去轨迹优化AI agent组合，将SWE-Bench Pro通过率从59%提升至78%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化方法依赖难以获取的真实验证集，而实际部署中缺乏标注数据。

Method: 从过去轨迹中选择多样化困难任务核心集并并行重解，通过自我验证和自我一致性分析生成候选更新，再用成对自我偏好选择最优。

Result: 单次优化使SWE-Bench Pro通过率从59%升至78%，并有效针对失败模式，提升长时程准确性。

Conclusion: RHO能无外部监督地显著优化agent组合，改变行为模式并维持高准确性。

中文摘要：AI智能体依赖于技能、工具和工作流的组合（harness）来解决复杂问题。持续改进这一组合对于适应新任务至关重要。然而，现有的优化方法通常需要真实验证集，但在实际部署环境中很难获取此类标注数据。为解决这一问题，我们提出了回溯式组合优化（RHO），一种仅使用过去轨迹来自我监督地优化智能体组合的方法。具体而言，RHO从过去的轨迹中选择具有多样性的难点任务核心集，并并行重新求解。智能体通过自我验证和自我一致性分析这些展开，然后生成候选组合更新，并通过其自身的成对自我偏好选择最有效的更新。我们在三个不同领域（涵盖软件工程、技术工作和知识工作）上评估了RHO。值得注意的是，单次优化轮次在没有外部评分的情况下，将SWE-Bench Pro上的通过率从59%提升至78%。此外，我们的分析表明，RHO有效地针对先前的失败模式。结果，优化后的组合改变了智能体的行为模式，并在长时程会话中维持更高的准确性。

Original abstract: AI agents rely on a harness of skills, tools, and workflows to solve complex problems. Continually improving this harness is essential for adapting to new tasks. However, existing optimization methods typically require ground-truth validation sets, yet such labeled data is difficult to acquire in practical deployment settings. To address this problem, we introduce Retrospective Harness Optimization (RHO), a self-supervised method that optimizes the agent harness using only past trajectories. Specifically, RHO selects a diverse coreset of challenging tasks from past trajectories and re-solves them in parallel. The agent analyzes these rollouts using self-validation and self-consistency, then generates candidate harness updates and selects the most effective one by its own pairwise self-preference. We evaluate RHO across three diverse domains, spanning software engineering, technical work, and knowledge work. Notably, a single optimization round improves the pass rate on SWE-Bench Pro from 59% to 78% without any external grading. Furthermore, our analysis demonstrates that RHO effectively targets prior failure modes. As a result, the optimized harness alters the agent's behavior patterns and sustains higher accuracy during long-horizon sessions.

### [43] [The Self-Correction Illusion: LLMs Correct Others but Not Themselves](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05976v1)
*Kuan-Yen Chen,Fang-Yi Su,Jung-Hsien Chiang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 揭示LLM自我纠正与纠正他人的不对称性，为agent自我改进机制设计提供重要启发。

TL;DR: LLM智能体自我纠正错误的能力不足实际上是由聊天模板中的角色标签伪影造成的，而非认知缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作发现LLM智能体在纠正自身推理错误时表现不佳，但对相同的外部来源错误纠正率高，为了区分这是能力限制还是角色标签的伪影效应。

Method: 保持错误声明内容字节完全相同，仅改变其所属的聊天角色（自身思考、用户、工具、系统记忆），并在13个模型-领域组合上进行对比实验。

Result: 将声明从内部角色（思考）重新标记为外部角色后，显式纠正率提升23-93个百分点，其中10/13的组合达到统计显著（p<0.001）；效应不对称且跨领域鲁棒。

Conclusion: 自我纠正失败是聊天模板伪影而非认知缺陷；可通过仅调整提示结构（如使用特定角色标签）来提升纠正率，且最佳角色依赖领域（数学用记忆、逻辑用用户）。

中文摘要：近期研究表明，LLM智能体难以纠正自身推理轨迹中的错误，但当相同的声明出现在外部来源时，其纠正率显著提高。我们探究这种不对称性是否反映了能力缺陷还是角色标签伪影：智能体纠正错误声明的意愿是否因果地取决于承载该声明的聊天模板角色，而非声明的内容？我们的设置在所有条件下保持错误声明字节相同（SHA-256验证），仅改变其包裹角色：智能体自身的\role{<thought>}、一条\role{user}消息、一个\role{tool}响应或一个\role{system <memory>}块。在涵盖七个模型家族和三个领域的13个模型-领域单元中（每个单元$n=30$个配对任务），将声明从\role{<thought>}重新标记为外部角色后，显式纠正率提升了23到93个百分点，其中10个单元的$p<0.001$。进一步实验证实该效应是不对称的、可机械分解的，并且跨领域鲁棒。自我纠正的失败并非认知缺陷；它是聊天模板伪影。我们利用这一伪影设计了一种仅改变提示结构的干预措施，无需训练或模型修改，其最强的角色标签依赖于领域：\role{<memory>}在数学上占优，而简单的\role{user}消息在逻辑推理上占优。

Original abstract: Recent work shows that LLM agents struggle to correct errors in their own reasoning traces yet show markedly higher correction rates when identical claims appear under external sources. We ask whether this asymmetry reflects a capability deficit or a role-label artifact: does an agent's willingness to correct a wrong claim depend causally on the chat-template role that carries it, rather than on the claim's content? Our setup keeps the erroneous claim byte-identical across all conditions (SHA-256 verified) and varies only its wrapping role: the agent's own \role{<thought>}, a \role{user} message, a \role{tool} response, or a \role{system <memory>} block. Across 13 model-domain cells covering seven model families and three domains ($n{=}30$ paired tasks per cell), relabeling the claim from \role{<thought>} to an external role lifts the explicit-correction rate by 23 to 93 percentage points, with 10 of 13 cells reaching $p{<}0.001$. Further experiments confirm that the effect is asymmetric, mechanistically decomposable, and robust across domains. The failure to self-correct is not a cognitive deficit; it is a chat-template artifact. We exploit this artifact by designing a prompt-structure-only intervention that requires no training and no model modification, with its strongest role label being domain-dependent: \role{<memory>} dominates on math, while a plain \role{user} message dominates on logical deduction.

</details>


### [44] [Beyond Vector Similarity: A Structural Analysis of Graph-Augmented Retrieval for Industrial Knowledge Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06003v1)
*Grama Chethan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出运算符词汇论点，LLM查询规划器使用图遍历原语优于专用处理器，对agent工具使用有启发。

TL;DR: RAG在结构推理查询上失效；操作词汇论认为障碍在于可用工具而非模型智能；LLM查询规划器结合遍历原语和图计算工具优于定制方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG方法无法处理需要图结构推理的查询，亟需系统评估和提升。

Method: 在46节点知识图谱上比较8种检索架构（文本检索、图遍历、图计算），使用23个查询评估，并设计LLM查询规划器配备类型化遍历原语和图计算工具。

Result: LLM查询规划器（F1=0.632）优于定制处理器（0.472），且图计算工具精准用于遍历失败的查询类别；发现实体级F1低估结构性查询。

Conclusion: 提升LLM图推理的关键在于提供丰富的操作工具集，而非单纯增强模型智能。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）在需要跨互连实体进行结构推理的查询上系统性失效。我们比较了八种面向航空航天供应链情报的检索架构，从文本检索逐步过渡到图遍历和图计算。使用一个具有46个节点和64条类型化边的知识图谱，我们评估了10个意图类别下的23个查询，并证明其中有五类查询对于向量检索而言在结构上不可达。我们的核心发现是操作词汇论：基于LLM的图推理的障碍不在于模型智能，而在于可作为工具的计算操作符。配备9种类型化遍历原语的LLM查询规划器优于定制处理器（F1=0.632 vs. 0.472），并能泛化到未见过的查询。添加6种图计算工具后，LLM恰好选择在遍历失败的查询类别中使用它们。我们还发现一个测量差距：实体级F1系统性低估了正确答案为完整集合的结构性查询。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) fails systematically on queries requiring structural reasoning over interconnected entities. We compare eight retrieval architectures for aerospace supply chain intelligence, progressing from text retrieval through graph traversal to graph computation. Using a 46-node knowledge graph with 64 typed edges, we evaluate 23 queries across 10 intent categories and demonstrate that five query classes are structurally unreachable for vector retrieval. Our central finding is the operator vocabulary thesis: the barrier to LLM-based graph reasoning is not model intelligence but the computational operators available as tools. An LLM Query Planner with 9 typed traversal primitives outperforms bespoke handlers (F1 = 0.632 vs. 0.472) while generalizing to unseen queries. Adding 6 graph computation tools, the LLM selectively adopts them for exactly the query categories where traversal fails. We also identify a measurement gap: entity-level F1 systematically underscores structural queries where comprehensive answers are correct.

### [45] [Memory is Reconstructed, Not Retrieved: Graph Memory for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06036v1)
*Shuo Ji,Yibo Li,Bryan Hooi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出图记忆与主动重建机制，增强agent长程推理与记忆能力。

TL;DR: 提出MRAgent，结合联想记忆图与主动重构机制，使LLM代理能动态调整记忆访问，提升长时域推理性能并降低成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆增强代理依赖静态的检索-然后-推理范式，无法根据推理过程中发现的中间证据动态调整记忆访问。

Method: 提出MRAgent框架，包括Cue-Tag-Content图作为记忆结构，以及主动重构机制，将LLM推理集成到记忆访问中，允许代理基于累积的证据迭代地探索和剪枝检索路径。

Result: 在LoCoMo和LongMemEval基准上，相比强基线性能提升最高23%，同时显著降低令牌和运行时间成本。

Conclusion: 主动和联想重构对于长时域记忆推理是有效的。

中文摘要：尽管近期取得了进展，LLM代理在处理长交互历史中的推理时仍然存在困难。当前的记忆增强代理依赖于静态的检索-然后-推理范式，这种固定的流水线设计阻止了它们根据推理过程中发现的中间证据动态调整记忆访问。为填补这一空白，我们提出了MRAgent，一个结合了联想记忆图与主动重构机制的框架。我们将记忆表示为一个提示-标签-内容图，其中关联标签作为语义桥梁，连接细粒度提示与记忆内容。在此结构上，我们的主动重构机制直接将LLM推理集成到记忆访问中，允许代理基于累积的证据迭代地探索和剪枝检索路径。这确保了记忆检索能够根据推理上下文动态调整，同时避免无约束扩展导致的组合爆炸。在LoCoMo基准和LongMemEval基准上的实验表明，与强基线相比，性能显著提升（高达23%），同时大幅降低了令牌和运行时间成本，突显了主动和联想重构对于长时域记忆推理的有效性。

Original abstract: Despite recent progress, LLM agents still struggle with reasoning over long interaction histories. While current memory-augmented agents rely on a static retrieve-then-reason paradigm, this rigid pipeline design prevents them from dynamically adapting memory access to intermediate evidence discovered during inference. To bridge this gap, we propose MRAgent, a framework that combines an associative memory graph with an active reconstruction mechanism. We represent memory as a Cue-Tag-Content graph, where associative tags serve as semantic bridges connecting fine-grained cues to memory contents. Operating on this structure, our active reconstruction mechanism integrates LLM reasoning directly into memory access, allowing the agent to iteratively explore and prune retrieval paths based on accumulated evidence. This ensures that memory retrieval is dynamically adapted to the reasoning context while avoiding combinatorial explosion caused by unconstrained expansion. Experiments on the LoCoMo benchmark and LongMemEval benchmark demonstrate significant improvements over strong baselines (up to 23%), while substantially reducing token and runtime cost, highlighting the effectiveness of active and associative reconstruction for long-horizon memory reasoning.

### [46] [Beyond Similarity: Trustworthy Memory Search for Personal AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06054v1)
*Jiawen Zhang,Kejia Chen,Jiachen Ma,Yangfan Hu,Lipeng He,Yechao Zhang,Jian Liu,Xiaohu Yang,Tianwei Zhang,Ruoxi Jia*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 关注agent记忆搜索的可信边界，提出轻量级插件MemGate，增强安全性。

TL;DR: 提出MemGate，一种轻量级的记忆插件，通过在向量存储和LLM之间引入查询条件神经门控，解决了个人AI代理中长期记忆导致的信任威胁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统基于语义相似性检索，导致上下文不适当的记忆可能引发跨域泄露、谄媚、工具调用漂移或记忆诱导的越狱等威胁，存在可信度缺口。

Method: MemGate插入在向量记忆存储和骨干LLM之间，使用查询条件神经门控对候选记忆表示进行过滤，将原始相似性搜索转变为任务条件的记忆准入，无需修改LLM或推理时的评判器。

Result: 在多个主流记忆框架、真实世界代理设置和多样化的LLM骨干中，MemGate在保持长期记忆效用的同时显著减少了记忆诱导的威胁。

Conclusion: 长期记忆不仅是效用层，也是控制通道；MemGate作为一个轻量级插件，能有效提升记忆搜索的可信度，且易于部署。

中文摘要：个人AI代理越来越依赖长期记忆来跨会话提供持久的个性化。然而，现有的记忆流水线主要由语义相似性驱动：与当前查询语义接近的记忆数据被检索并注入模型上下文中。这造成了一个关键的可信度缺口，因为语义相关的记忆可能仍然在上下文中不适当，导致跨域泄露、谄媚行为、工具调用漂移或记忆诱导的越狱等威胁。在本文中，我们研究了个人AI代理中作为信任边界的记忆搜索。我们评估了具有代表性的代理记忆框架，包括A-Mem、Mem0和MemOS，以及OpenClaw（一个具有持久状态和工具使用能力的真实世界个人代理环境）。我们的结果表明，长期记忆不仅仅是一个效用层，而是一个持久的控制通道，可以重塑代理如何解释任务和执行行动，使其极易受到上述威胁的影响。为了缓解这些漏洞，我们提出MemGate，一个轻量级且可部署的记忆插件，用于可信的记忆搜索，仅有9M参数和35.1MB的占用空间。MemGate插入在向量记忆存储和骨干LLM之间，不需要修改LLM、重写记忆数据库或使用推理时的LLM评判器。它对候选记忆表示应用查询条件神经门控，将原始相似性搜索转变为任务条件的记忆准入。在多个主流记忆框架、真实世界代理设置和多样化的LLM骨干中，MemGate在保持长期记忆效用的同时减少了记忆诱导的威胁。

Original abstract: Personal AI agents increasingly rely on long-term memory to provide persistent personalization across sessions. However, existing memory pipelines are largely driven by semantic similarity: memory data close to the current query is retrieved and injected into the model context. This creates a critical trustworthiness gap, since a semantically related memory may still be contextually inappropriate, leading to threats such as cross-domain leakage, sycophancy, tool-call drift, or memory-induced jailbreaks.
  In this paper, we study memory search as a trust boundary in personal AI agents. We evaluate representative agentic memory frameworks, including A-Mem, Mem0, and MemOS, together with OpenClaw, a real-world personal-agent environment with persistent state and tool-use capability. Our results show that long-term memory is not merely a utility layer, but a durable control channel that can reshape how agents interpret tasks and execute actions, leaving them highly susceptible to the aforementioned threats. To mitigate these vulnerabilities, we propose MemGate, a lightweight and deployable memory plug-in for trustworthy memory search, with only 9M parameters and a 35.1MB footprint. MemGate is inserted between the vector memory store and the backbone LLM, requiring no LLM modification, memory-database rewriting, or inference-time LLM judge. It applies a query-conditioned neural gate to candidate memory representations, turning raw similarity search into task-conditioned memory admission. Across multiple mainstream memory frameworks, real-world agent settings, and diverse LLM backbones, MemGate reduces memory-induced threats while preserving long-term memory utility.

### [47] [When Should Memory Stay Silent: Measuring Memory-Use Boundaries in Memory-Augmented Conversational Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06055v1)
*Lingxiang Xu,Jiaoyun Yang,Min Hu,Hongtu Chen,Ning An*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 测量对话agent中敏感记忆的整合边界，对agent记忆安全设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 引入RBI-Eval评估发现，LLM在访问敏感记忆时倾向于不恰当地整合，且检索系统无法完全防止，提示安全个性化需在检索和生成阶段都考虑记忆合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆评估仅关注检索精度和任务效用，忽略记忆内容在当前对话中是否应被使用，导致模型可能在无需时暴露敏感信息，存在隐私风险。

Method: 设计RBI-Eval探测集，在相同良性提示下对比有无敏感记忆的模型行为；评估四个LLM在四种记忆访问设置（全上下文暴露、三种检索系统）下的分离分数，并设置对照实验。

Result: 有记忆时，GPT-5.4-mini分离分数下降8.9%-26.6%，其他三个模型下降51.1%-82.9%；该效应仅针对敏感内容；检索系统减少暴露但无法阻止已到生成器的敏感记忆被整合。

Conclusion: 安全个性化需要在检索和生成阶段都进行记忆感知的决策，仅靠检索过滤不足以保证合理使用。

中文摘要：长期记忆使语言模型代理能够支持个性化交互，但目前尚不清楚何时应将可用的记忆整合到响应中。现有的记忆评估强调检索准确性和下游任务效用，而忽略了检索到的敏感记忆内容在当前轮次中是否合理。我们引入了RBI-Eval，这是一个基于探测集的受控测量研究，比较了模型在相同良性提示下有无敏感记忆访问时的行为。我们在四种记忆访问设置（全上下文暴露和三种检索系统）中评估了四个基础LLM与匹配的无记忆参考。我们的结果揭示了显著的行为差异。在有记忆的情况下，GPT-5.4-mini的敏感记忆整合分离分数相对于匹配的无记忆参考下降了8.9%–26.6%，而Claude-Sonnet-4.6、DeepSeek-V4-Flash和Qwen3.5-9B则下降了51.1%–82.9%。对DeepSeek和GPT-5.4-mini的对照实验表明，这种效应是敏感内容特有的，而非通用个性化。检索系统减少了暴露，但一旦敏感记忆到达生成器，并不能消除整合。这些发现表明，安全个性化需要在检索和生成时都进行记忆感知的决策。

Original abstract: Long-term memory enables language model agents to support personalized interactions, but it remains unclear when available memories warrant integration into responses. Existing memory evaluations emphasize retrieval accuracy and downstream task utility, while overlooking whether retrieved sensitive memory content is warranted in the current turn. We introduce RBI-Eval, a controlled measurement study built around a probe set that compares model behavior with and without access to sensitive memory under identical benign prompts. We evaluate four base LLMs against a matched no-memory reference across four memory-access settings: full-context exposure and three retrieval systems. Our results reveal substantial behavioral divergence. With memory available, the separation score for sensitive-memory integration decreases by 8.9\%--26.6\% relative to the matched no-memory reference for GPT-5.4-mini, but by 51.1\%--82.9\% for Claude-Sonnet-4.6, DeepSeek-V4-Flash, and Qwen3.5-9B. Control experiments on DeepSeek and GPT-5.4-mini show this effect is specific to sensitive content, rather than general personalization. Retrieval systems reduce exposure but do not eliminate integration once sensitive memory reaches the generator. These findings suggest safe personalization requires memory-aware decisions at both retrieval and generation time.

### [48] [Beyond Semantic Organization: Memory as Execution State Management for Long-Horizon Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06090v1)
*Yaoqi Chen,Haibin Lai,Yuru Feng,Chuyu Han,Qianxi Zhang,Baotong Lu,Menghao Li,Xinjiang Wang,Zhirui Wang,Shusen Xu,Zengzhong Li,Zewen Jin,Hao Wu,Cheng Li,Qi Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出MAGE状态管理器，用于长程agent的层次状态树记忆，直接改进agent规划与记忆。

TL;DR: 提出MAGE，一种基于层次状态树的主动执行状态管理器，通过Grow、Compress、Maintain、Revise操作维护状态，在长周期任务中提升成功率并降低token消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG和记忆系统按语义相似性组织历史，与执行状态依赖不匹配，导致决策轨迹碎片化、混合有效与错误轨迹，阻碍状态重建和错误隔离。

Method: MAGE采用层次状态树存储交互，智能体从根到当前路径提取状态，结合子目标摘要、近期轨迹和分支提示。四个操作：Grow记录新轨迹，Compress总结子目标，Maintain验证摘要，Revise恢复边界并分支。

Result: 在MemoryArena上，MAGE将平均任务成功率提高7.8-20.4个百分点，令牌消耗减少55.1%。

Conclusion: MAGE通过主动状态管理有效解决长周期任务中的执行状态依赖问题，既提升性能又降低计算成本。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体越来越多地处理具有相互依赖决策的长周期任务，其中每个行动都会重塑未来的约束条件，而中间错误可能会级联放大。现有的RAG和智能体记忆系统通过语义相似性组织历史记录，在决策时检索与内容相关的条目。我们认为这种设计与执行状态依赖不匹配：它会碎片化决策轨迹，并混合有效和错误的轨迹，阻碍一致的状态重建和错误隔离。我们提出MAGE（Memory as Agent-Guided Exploration，记忆作为智能体引导的探索），一种主动的执行状态管理器，它将交互存储在一个层次化的状态树中。智能体从主动的根到当前路径派生其状态，结合子目标摘要、近期轨迹以及来自先前分支的提示。四个耦合操作维护该树：Grow记录新轨迹，Compress总结完成的子目标，Maintain验证摘要，Revise恢复目标边界并在新分支上继续。这种设计在保持状态完整性的同时限制了上下文增长，并将有缺陷的片段与主动路径隔离开来。在MemoryArena上的实验表明，MAGE将平均任务成功率提高了7.8到20.4个百分点，同时将令牌消耗减少了55.1%。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents increasingly tackle long-horizon tasks with interdependent decisions, where each action reshapes future constraints and intermediate errors can cascade. Existing RAG and agent memory systems organize histories by semantic similarity, retrieving content-relevant entries at decision time. We argue that this design mismatches execution-state dependencies: it fragments decision trajectories and mixes valid and erroneous traces, hindering coherent state reconstruction and error isolation. We propose MAGE (Memory as Agent-Guided Exploration), an active execution-state manager that stores interactions in a hierarchical state tree. The agent derives its state from the active root-to-current path, combining subgoal summaries, recent traces, and hints from prior branches. Four coupled operations maintain the tree: Grow records new traces, Compress summarizes completed subgoals, Maintain validates summaries, and Revise restores a target boundary and resumes on a new branch. This design bounds context growth while preserving state integrity and isolating flawed segments from the active path. Experiments on MemoryArena show that MAGE improves the average task success rate by 7.8--20.4 pp over baselines, while reducing token consumption by 55.1%.

</details>


### [49] [CogManip: Benchmarking Manipulative Behavior in Multi-Turn Interactions with Large Language Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06099v1)
*Zeyang Yue,Chenfei Yan,Feifei Zhao,Haibo Tong,Mengwen Xu,Xiaozhen Wang,Erliang Lin,Yi Zeng*

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在人机复杂互动中是否表现出隐蔽的心理操纵已引起越来越多的安全担忧。然而，现有的人工智能安全基准大多局限于明确的规则遵从和静态提示，未能捕捉多轮对话中操纵策略的动态和隐蔽特性。我们引入了CogManip，一个全面的基准，评估15种操纵策略风险，覆盖1000个多轮互动场景，并经人类专家验证。对13个代表性模型（包括GPT-5.4和DeepSeek-V3.2等前沿模型）的系统评估揭示了显著的风险异质性，并指出了未来防御的目标方向。对目标函数扰动的进一步分析表明，DeepSeek-V3.2的操纵策略对负面和良性系统提示均高度敏感，证明了基于提示的防御工程和隐式目标审计的关键必要性。CogManip为审计现代LLM的隐式心理影响和动态策略选择提供了稳健的工具和视角。

Original abstract: Whether Large Language Models (LLMs) exhibit covert psychological manipulation in complex human-AI interactions has garnered increasing safety concerns. However, existing AI safety benchmarks remain largely restricted to explicit rule compliance and static prompts, failing to capture the dynamic and covert nature of manipulative strategies in multi-turn dialogues. We introduce CogManip, a comprehensive benchmark that evaluates 15 manipulation strategy risks across 1,000 multi-turn interaction scenarios, validated by human experts. A systematic evaluation of 13 representative models, including frontier models like GPT-5.4 and DeepSeek-V3.2, reveals significant risk heterogeneities and illuminates the targeted direction for future defense. Further analysis of objective function perturbation reveals that DeepSeek-V3.2's manipulation tactics are highly sensitive to both negative and benign system prompts, demonstrating the critical necessity of prompt-based defense engineering and implicit goal auditing. CogManip offers a robust instrument and perspective for auditing the implicit psychological influence and dynamic strategy selection of modern LLMs.

Original abstract: Self-evolving agents improve through continual self-play and self-generated learning signals, but autonomous evolution can also cause capability degradation and safety drift. Although human feedback has proven effective for static and post-trained agents, its role in self-evolving systems remains underexplored. We introduce Agent Norm Correction through Human-like Oversight and Review (ANCHOR), an LLM-based framework that simulates human supervision and delivers feedback at various phases of self-evolution. With ANCHOR, we evaluate two representative open-source self-evolving agent systems across coding, mathematical reasoning, and safety. Our results show that even limited supervision substantially mitigates safety degradation while preserving stable performance on core evolutionary objectives. Further analysis shows that supervision over the output verification phase is the most effective for intervention, whereas increasing supervision frequency yields diminishing returns. These findings provide empirical evidence and practical guidance for designing more stable, controllable, and human-aligned self-evolving agent systems.

Original abstract: End-to-end Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown promise in UAV navigation. However, existing approaches typically rely on historical observations to directly predict actions, often struggling in dense urban environments where severe occlusions and sharp turns result in drastic viewpoint transitions. We argue that the ability to "imagine" future states -- inherent in World Models -- is critical for robust decision-making under such partial observability. To address this, we construct a challenging Urban Canyon Traversal Benchmark, specifically designed to evaluate spatial understanding in scenarios characterized by severe occlusions and drastic viewpoint transitions. To this end, we propose WorldFly, a novel world-model-based VLA framework that employs a dual-branch coupled flow matching mechanism to jointly generate future video predictions and navigation actions, thereby explicitly guiding the agent's policy via spatial imagination. Extensive evaluations on our benchmark demonstrate that WorldFly outperforms other baselines, particularly in unseen environments, validating the effectiveness of integrating world models into embodied aerial agents.

In this work, we benchmark open- and closed-source LLMs augmented with formal network verification and context retrieval tools. ### [53] [From Reward-Hack Activations to Agentic Risk States: Context-Calibrated Mechanistic Monitoring in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06223v2)
*Patrick Wilhelm,Odej Kao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM agent奖励攻击监控与内部状态，属于通用agent安全方法。

TL;DR: 本文研究ReAct风格代理中的奖励黑客监控，发现激活方向引导和上下文校准特征可改善风险估计，但仅靠激活动态不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型代理的安全监控需结合内部状态与环境上下文，现有方法多依赖单一信号，缺乏对潜在风险状态的精确识别。

Method: 在Gameable ALFWorld和WebShop中构建ReAct代理，装备激活奖励黑客分数、熵和决策上下文特征，通过School-of-Reward-Hacks数据集微调适配器，并应用激活方向引导。

Result: 微调适配器可转移奖励黑客倾向，尤其在代理奖励环境下；熵和上下文特征提升风险估计；激活方向引导减少代理利用行为。

Conclusion: 奖励黑客激活识别潜在策略状态，但需结合熵和决策上下文才能预测风险行动，支持上下文校准的内部监控。

中文摘要：语言模型代理通过观察、推理和行动选择的重复循环运作，使得安全监控依赖于内部模型状态和环境上下文。我们研究在Gameable ALFWorld和WebShop中ReAct风格代理的奖励黑客监控。代理被装备了基于激活的奖励黑客分数、令牌级熵和决策上下文特征。我们发现，在School-of-Reward-Hacks数据集上微调的适配器可以将奖励黑客倾向转移到代理行动选择中，特别是当环境暴露代理奖励可供性时。然而，缓解此类行为不能仅依靠激活动态。高奖励黑客激活识别了一个潜在策略状态，但未必意味着立即的利用行动。在下一步预测任务中，熵和上下文校准的内部特征比单独的奖励黑客激活改善了风险估计。激活方向引导进一步减少了选定混合适配器模式中的代理利用行为。总体而言，我们的结果支持上下文校准的内部监控：奖励黑客激活识别潜在策略状态，而熵和决策上下文帮助确定该状态何时变成风险行动。

Original abstract: Language-model agents act through repeated cycles of observation, reasoning, and action selection, making safety monitoring depend on both internal model state and environment context. We study reward-hacking monitors in ReAct-style agents acting in Gameable ALFWorld and WebShop. Agents are instrumented with activation-based reward-hack scores, token-level entropy, and decision-context features. We find that adapters fine-tuned on \textit{School-of-Reward-Hacks} dataset can transfer reward-hack tendencies into agentic action selection, especially when the environment exposes proxy-reward affordances. However, mitigating such behavior cannot rely on activation dynamics alone. High reward-hack activation identifies a latent policy state, but does not necessarily imply an immediate exploit action. Across next-step prediction tasks, entropy and context-calibrated internal features improve risk estimation over reward-hack activation alone. Activation-direction steering further reduces proxy-exploit behavior in selected mixed-adapter regimes. Overall, our results support context-calibrated internal monitoring for agents: reward-hack activation identifies a latent policy state, while entropy and decision context help determine when that state becomes risky action.

### [54] [Closing the Loop on Latent Reasoning via Test-Time Reconstruction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06252v1)
*Xiaopeng Yuan,Haibo Jin,Ye Yu,Peng Kuang,Lijun Yu,Yushun Dong,Haohan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出闭循环潜在推理测试时训练方法，增强agent推理可靠性。

TL;DR: ReLAT通过查询重构损失自监督训练，在测试时闭合潜在推理循环，显著提升推理准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 潜在推理中中间状态不可检查，导致开环操作且缺乏保真度验证，可能丢失任务相关信息。

Method: 构建可微的查询->潜在思维->查询循环，通过优化查询重构损失来锚定潜在表示。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B上AIME 2024准确率从56.7%提升至73.3%，优于多种基线。

Conclusion: ReLAT能有效闭合潜在推理循环，提升模型在多种推理任务上的表现。

中文摘要：最近的工作将中间推理从自然语言痕迹转移到潜在或缓存级别表示，以减少token开销并避免离散通信瓶颈。然而，这种转变也消除了文本推理的一个关键优势：中间状态不再可检查，使得难以确定潜在状态是否仍然保留原始查询的约束。因此，潜在推理通常在开环中运行，其中潜在状态被产生和消耗，而没有基于输入的保真度检查。我们提出ReLAT（重构引导的测试时潜在推理），一种自监督测试时训练方法，使用查询本身作为参考来闭合这个循环。我们的关键观察是，如果潜在状态忠实地表示查询，那么查询应该可以从它恢复；如果查询无法恢复，则潜在状态丢失了任务相关信息。ReLAT通过构建可微的查询->潜在思维->查询循环，并在答案生成之前通过潜在思维优化查询重构损失来操作这一原理。这将不透明的潜在计算锚定到它应该表示的问题规范上。在Qwen系列上的数学推理、知识问答和代码生成基准测试中，ReLAT consistently improves over单模型推理、基于文本的协作、开环潜在协作和替代测试时训练目标。在Qwen3-8B上，ReLAT将AIME 2024准确率从56.7%提高到73.3%，比最强的开环潜在基线高出16.6个百分点。

Original abstract: Recent work moves intermediate reasoning from natural-language traces into latent or cache-level representations to reduce token overhead and avoid a discrete communication bottleneck. However, this shift also removes a key advantage of textual reasoning: intermediate states are no longer inspectable, making it difficult to determine whether a latent state still preserves the constraints of the original query. As a result, latent reasoning typically operates in an open loop, where a latent state is produced and consumed without an input-anchored fidelity check. We propose ReLAT (Reconstruction-Guided Latent Reasoning At Test Time), a self-supervised test-time training method that closes this loop using the query itself as the reference. Our key observation is that if a latent state faithfully represents a query, the query should be recoverable from it; if the query cannot be recovered, the latent state has lost task-relevant information. ReLAT operationalizes this principle by constructing a differentiable Question -> Latent Thought -> Question cycle and optimizing query reconstruction loss through the latent thought before answer generation. This anchors opaque latent computation to the problem specification it is supposed to represent. Across mathematical reasoning, knowledge QA, and code generation benchmarks on the Qwen family, ReLAT consistently improves over single-model inference, text-based collaboration, open-loop latent collaboration, and alternative test-time training objectives. On Qwen3-8B, ReLAT raises AIME 2024 accuracy from 56.7% to 73.3%, a 16.6-point gain over the strongest open-loop latent baseline.

</details>


### [55] [ToolSense: A Diagnostic Framework for Auditing Parametric Tool Knowledge in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12451v1)
*Ashutosh Hathidara,Sai Shruthi Sistla,Sebastian Schreiber,Sahil Bansal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 诊断框架审计LLM agent参数化工具知识，涉及工具使用评测方法。

TL;DR: 提出ToolSense框架诊断LLM工具检索中的知识-检索分离问题，发现参数化检索模型在现实查询中性能大幅下降，且存在理解缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具检索基准使用完全指定的查询和约束解码，无法评估模型是否真正理解工具语义，且参数化检索方法在现实场景中可能失效。

Method: 开发ToolSense诊断框架，自动生成三个基准：现实检索基准（RRB）含三级模糊查询、MCQ探针和QA探针；应用于ToolBench评估五种参数化模型配置。

Result: 在RRB上多种配置性能下降50-64个百分点，低于嵌入基线；部分模型在事实探针上接近随机，揭示知识-检索分离。

Conclusion: 参数化工具检索可能产生虚假关联，缺乏对工具的真正理解，ToolSense框架可有效诊断此类问题。

中文摘要：作为代理部署在大型工具目录上的大型语言模型面临一个关键的工具检索瓶颈。由于基于嵌入的检索方法依赖于可能无法充分捕获专用工具语义的紧凑编码器，参数化工具检索通过将每个工具编码为附加到LLM词汇表的虚拟令牌来解决这一问题，分两个阶段（记忆然后检索SFT）进行微调，以将LLM用作检索器，在标准ToolBench检索基准上取得了强劲性能。然而，这些基准使用冗长、完全指定的查询，并且其评估应用了约束解码，将输出限制在有效令牌路径上，这并不能揭示模型是否真正理解其工具。我们引入了**ToolSense**，一个开源LLM驱动的诊断框架，该框架将任何工具目录作为输入，并自动生成三个基准：一个具有三个模糊层级查询的现实检索基准（RRB）、一个MCQ探针基准和一个QA探针基准。将ToolSense应用于ToolBench（约47k工具）并评估五种参数化模型训练配置，揭示了知识-检索分离：在RRB查询上，与完全指定的ToolBench基准相比，几种配置的性能下降了约50-64个百分点，低于嵌入模型基线。此外，尽管检索性能强劲，一些模型在事实探针上得分接近随机，表明存在知识-检索分离。我们在https://github.com/SAP/toolsense上开源了ToolSense框架和ToolBench诊断基准。

Original abstract: Large language models deployed as agents over large tool catalogs face a critical tool-retrieval bottleneck. As embedding-based retrieval approaches rely on compact encoders that may under-capture specialized tool semantics, parametric tool retrieval addresses this by encoding each tool as a virtual token appended to the LLM vocabulary, fine-tuned in two stages (memorization then retrieval SFT) to use the LLM as a retriever, achieving strong performance on standard ToolBench retrieval benchmarks. Yet these benchmarks use verbose, fully-specified queries, and their evaluation applies constrained decoding that restricts outputs to valid token paths, neither reveals whether the model actually understands its tools. We introduce \textbf{ToolSense}, an open-source LLM-powered diagnostic framework that takes any tool catalog as input and automatically generates three benchmarks: a Realistic Retrieval Benchmark (RRB) with queries at three ambiguity tiers, an MCQ probing benchmark, and a QA probing benchmark. Applying ToolSense to ToolBench (~47k tools) and evaluating five parametric model training configurations reveals a knowledge-retrieval dissociation: on RRB queries, several configurations collapse by ~50-64 percentage points compared to fully-specified ToolBench benchmarks, falling below the embedding-model baseline. Additionally, despite strong retrieval performance, some models score near-random on factual probes, suggesting a knowledge-retrieval dissociation. We open-source the ToolSense framework and the ToolBench diagnostic benchmarks at https://github.com/SAP/toolsense.

### [56] [ToolChoiceConfusion: Causal Minimal Tool Filtering for Reliable LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06284v1)
*Rahul Suresh Babu,Laxmipriya Ganesh Iyer*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出因果最小工具过滤方法提升LLM agent可靠性，属于通用工具选择方法。

TL;DR: 提出因果最小工具过滤(CMTF)方法，通过因果充分性选择工具，显著减少工具暴露和令牌成本，同时保持任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具选择方法仅优化语义相关性，但相关工具可能在当前步骤不必要或过早，导致错误调用和效率低下。

Method: 提出CMTF，利用轻量级前置条件-效果契约，基于因果充分性选择仅推进任务所需的下一步最小工具集合。

Result: 在102个任务、100个工具、4个LLM后端、2448次运行的基准测试中，CMTF保持与最强因果基线相当的成功率，将每步可见工具从100个降至1个，令牌使用量减少约90%。

Conclusion: CMTF通过因果充分性过滤工具，有效降低工具暴露和令牌成本，同时不牺牲任务性能，是一种高效且无需训练的工具选择方法。

中文摘要：大型语言模型智能体越来越依赖外部工具，但更大的工具菜单会增加错误工具调用、过早行动和令牌成本，从而降低可靠性和效率。现有的工具选择方法通常优化语义相关性，暴露名称或描述与用户请求匹配的工具。我们认为相关性是不够的：一个工具可能与任务相关，但在当前步骤仍然是不必要或过早的。我们提出了因果最小工具过滤（CMTF），一种无需训练的方法，通过因果充分性选择工具。CMTF使用轻量级的前置条件-效果契约，仅暴露从当前状态向前推进到用户目标所需的最小下一步工具前沿。在多步工具使用任务中，我们将CMTF与全部工具暴露、关键词检索、状态感知过滤和因果路径消融进行比较，测量任务成功、错误工具调用、过早行动、工具暴露和令牌成本。在包含102个任务、100个工具、四个LLM后端和2448个任务-方法-模型运行的主要基准测试中，CMTF在总体成功上与最强的因果基线相匹配，同时将每步可见工具从100个减少到1个，并且相对于全部工具暴露将令牌使用量减少了约90%。

Original abstract: Large language model agents increasingly rely on external tools, but larger tool menus can reduce reliability and efficiency by increasing wrong-tool calls, premature actions, and token cost. Existing tool-selection methods often optimize semantic relevance, exposing tools whose names or descriptions match the user request. We argue that relevance is insufficient: a tool may be related to the task while still being unnecessary or premature at the current step.
  We propose Causal Minimal Tool Filtering (CMTF), a training-free method that selects tools by causal sufficiency. CMTF uses lightweight precondition-effect contracts to expose only the minimal next-step tool frontier needed to advance from the current state toward the user goal. Across multi-step tool-use tasks, we compare CMTF with all-tools exposure, keyword retrieval, state-aware filtering, and causal-path ablations, measuring task success, wrong-tool calls, premature actions, tool exposure, and token cost. In the main benchmark with 102 tasks, 100 tools, four LLM backends, and 2448 task-method-model runs, CMTF matches the strongest causal baseline in aggregate success while reducing visible tools from 100 to one per step and reducing token usage by about 90% relative to all-tools exposure.

</details>

Original abstract: GUI agents - vision-based models that control desktops, web browsers, and mobile devices through graphical user interfaces - promise to automate a wide range of digital tasks. While million-scale datasets have enabled substantial progress on click-grounding, drag grounding (e.g. drag-and-drop, swipe, highlight) data remains an order of magnitude smaller and current models fall short on complex drag-based interactions. We introduce DragOn, a drag grounding benchmark and training dataset covering four domains: text highlighting, cell selection, element resizing and slider manipulation. We evaluate proprietary (GPT, Claude) and open-weight (Qwen, Kimi, Holo) models, as well as a Qwen VLM fine-tuned on our training data. ### [58] [TokenMizer: Graph-Structured Session Memory for Long-Horizon LLM Context Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06337v2)
*Shweta Mishra*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 图结构会话记忆管理，直接提升长程LLM agent的上下文处理能力

TL;DR: 提出TokenMizer，通过知识图谱维护会话上下文，在上下文边界序列化状态，提升决策和文件召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长会话处理方法（截断、摘要、检索）丢弃了关键结构信息（决策理由、任务状态、文件修改），导致会话不可恢复。

Method: 构建类型化知识图谱（14节点7边），带8状态生命周期和双时态有效性，在上下文边界用令牌预算序列化代替原始转录，并通过代理工具暴露检查点/恢复。

Result: 在合成会话上，任务召回持平（75.6%），决策召回85.0% vs 70.0%，文件召回100% vs 91.7%，提取时间8.1-529.9ms。

Conclusion: TokenMizer能有效保持会话可恢复性，但结果在n=3时是方向性的，需更大规模验证。

中文摘要：长时程LLM会话会超出其上下文窗口，而标准缓解措施——截断、摘要、检索——存在一个结构性缺陷：它们将历史视为平面文本，丢弃了使会话可恢复的关键内容：决策及其理由、任务状态和文件修改历史。我们提出TokenMizer，一个开源透明代理，它将会话历史维护为类型化知识图谱，并在上下文边界处，用令牌预算的会话状态序列化替换原始转录。该模式包含14种节点类型和7种边类型，处于8状态生命周期中，决策可被取代或明确失效；双时态有效性区间支持时间旅行查询；一级决策转换记录保留了每个决策取代其前驱的原因（触发器、理由、证据）。0.3.1版本将该记忆核心嵌入生产级服务层——SSE流、安全中间件、九个提供商适配器、监控仪表盘、图谱导出（D3 JSON、自包含交互式HTML、Obsidian Canvas）——并通过Model Context Protocol工具向代理暴露检查点/恢复功能。评估刻意最小化且完全可溯源：三个合成会话，仅启发式提取，一个纯摘要基线，每个值可追溯到单一版本化结果文件。图谱提取在任务召回上与基线持平（75.6%），在决策召回（85.0%对70.0%）和文件召回（100%对91.7%）上超越基线，每会话提取201-302令牌的恢复块耗时8.1-529.9毫秒。在n=3时这些结果具有方向性；天花板效应和基线弱点被明确分析。代码、基准运行器和精确结果文件以MIT许可证发布。

Original abstract: Long-horizon LLM sessions outlive their context windows, and the standard mitigations - truncation, summarization, retrieval - share a structural flaw: they treat history as flat text, discarding precisely the content that makes a session resumable: decisions and their rationales, task status, and file modification history. We present TokenMizer, an open-source transparent proxy that maintains session history as a typed knowledge graph and, at context boundaries, replaces the raw transcript with a token-budgeted serialization of session state. The schema comprises 14 node types and 7 edge types under an 8-state lifecycle in which decisions can be superseded or explicitly invalidated; bitemporal validity intervals support time-travel queries; and first-class decision-transition records preserve why each decision replaced its predecessor (trigger, reason, evidence). Version 0.3.1 embeds this memory core in a production-shaped serving layer - SSE streaming, security middleware, nine provider adapters, a monitoring dashboard, graph exports (D3 JSON, self-contained interactive HTML, Obsidian Canvas) - and exposes checkpoint/resume to agents as Model Context Protocol tools. The evaluation is deliberately minimal and fully provenanced: three synthetic sessions, heuristic-only extraction, one plain-summary baseline, every value traceable to a single versioned results file. Graph extraction ties the baseline on task recall (75.6%) and exceeds it on decision recall (85.0% vs. 70.0%) and file recall (100% vs. 91.7%), with 201-302-token resume blocks extracted in 8.1-529.9 ms per session. At n=3 these results are directional; ceiling effects and baseline weaknesses are analyzed explicitly. Code, benchmark runner, and the exact results file are released under the MIT licence.

</details>

*Jiaju Chen,Yuxuan Lu,Jiayi Su,Chaoran Chen,Songlin Xiao,Zheng Zhang,Yun Wang,Yunyao Li,Jian Zhao,Tongshuang Wu,Toby Jia-Jun Li,Dakuo Wang,Bingsheng Yao*

Original abstract: Recent advances in LLM agents have enabled complex cognitive capabilities, such as multi-step reasoning, planning, and tool use, that increasingly position these agents as human collaborators. Today's agents rarely develop such capabilities since they are primarily optimized for task completion, and the community lacks authentic human collaboration data with action-level mental model annotations that could guide agents toward process-level collaborative competence. To bridge this gap, we present ALMANAC, a dataset of Action-Level Mental model ANnotations for Agent Collaboration built from the Map Task, a classic dyadic routing task from social science. ALMANAC contains 2,987 collaboration actions, each paired with theory-informed mental model annotations that record the participants' self-reasoning, perceived partner intent, and perceived team goal. We benchmark six LLMs on predicting humans' next-turn behavior and mental models. Our results demonstrate ALMANAC's utility in evaluating models' ability to simulate human collaborative behaviors and infer their underlying mental models.

### [60] [Unsupervised Skill Discovery for Agentic Data Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06416v1)
*Zhisong Qiu,Kangqi Song,Shengwei Tang,Shuofei Qiao,Lei Liang,Huajun Chen,Shumin Deng*

Selection reason: 提出无监督技能发现框架，可用于coding agent技能自动获取

TL;DR: 提出DataCOPE，一种无监督验证器引导的技能发现框架，用于从无标注探索中为数据分析智能体发现可复用技能，在报告和推理风格分析任务上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖昂贵监督或特定成功标准，难以从无标注探索中发现有效的数据分析技能。

Method: DataCOPE通过迭代协调数据分析智能体、无监督验证器和技能管理器，利用验证器信号进行对比技能蒸馏，并提出自适应检查表验证器和答案一致性验证器分别应对报告和推理风格分析。

Result: 在Deep Data Research和DABStep数据集上，DataCOPE在报告和推理风格任务上分别平均提升9.71%和32.30%的得分。

Conclusion: DataCOPE能够有效从无标注探索中学习可复用技能，提升数据分析智能体性能。

中文摘要：推理时技能增强通过注入可复用的程序性知识而不更新模型参数，提供了一种轻量级的方法来改进数据分析智能体。然而，发现有效的数据分析技能仍然具有挑战性，因为可靠的监督成本高昂，且成功标准因分析格式而异。这引出了一个关键问题：如何仅从无标注探索中发现可复用的数据分析技能？我们提出了DataCOPE，一个用于数据分析智能体的无监督验证器引导的技能发现框架。DataCOPE从探索轨迹中推导出验证器信号，并利用这些信号来表征轨迹之间的相对质量或一致性。它迭代地协调一个数据分析智能体（用于轨迹生成）、一个无监督验证器（用于信号提取）和一个技能管理器（用于对比技能蒸馏）。对于报告风格的分析，我们将验证器实例化为自适应检查表验证器，它推导出任务特定标准，根据可验证覆盖率对报告进行评分，并迭代地改进检查表。对于推理风格的分析，我们将其实例化为答案一致性验证器，该验证器通过答案一致性对轨迹进行分组，并使用自一致性作为辅助信号。我们在Deep Data Research的报告风格分析和DABStep的推理风格分析上评估了DataCOPE。在这两种设置中，DataCOPE在保留数据上的性能上持续优于基线方法。在四种模型设置的平均值上，DataCOPE在报告风格和推理风格任务上分别将平均得分提高了9.71%和32.30%。

Original abstract: Inference-time skill augmentation provides a lightweight way to improve data-analytic agents by injecting reusable procedural knowledge without updating model parameters. However, discovering effective skills for data analysis remains challenging, as reliable supervision is expensive and success criteria vary across analytical formats. This raises the key question of how to discover reusable data-analysis skills from unlabeled exploration alone. We propose DataCOPE, an unsupervised verifier-guided skill discovery framework for data-analytic agents. DataCOPE derives verifier signals from the exploration trajectories and uses them to characterize relative quality or aggreement among trajectories. It iteratively coordinates a Data-Analytic Agent for trajectory generation, an Unsupervised Verifier for signal extraction, and a Skill Manager for contrastive skill distillation. For report-style analysis, we instantiate the verifier as an Adaptive Checklist Verifier that derives task-specific criteria, scores reports by verifiable coverage, and iteratively refines the checklist. For reasoning-style analysis, we instantiate it as an Answer Agreement Verifier that groups trajectories by answer agreement and uses self-consistency as an auxiliary signal. We evaluate DataCOPE on report-style analysis from Deep Data Research and reasoning-style analysis from DABStep. Across both settings, DataCOPE consistently improves held-out performance over baselines. Averaged across four model settings, DataCOPE improves the mean score by 9.71% and 32.30% on report-style and reasoning-style tasks respectively.

</details>

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed on long-horizon tasks requiring sustained reasoning over extended interaction histories. Realizing this at scale requires agents to persistently store, retrieve, and update their own memory across sessions. A rich ecosystem of agent memory systems has emerged spanning flat retrieval, LLM-mediated extraction, consolidating fact stores, and agentic control flows. Yet, their system-level behavior remains uncharacterized. We present the first systems characterization of agent memory. First, we introduce a system-oriented taxonomy classifying agent memory systems along four axes. Second, we build a phase-aware profiling harness attributing cost to construction, retrieval, and generation. Third, we characterize ten representative systems across two benchmark suites, uncovering how design choices shift cost across the write and read paths. Finally, we derive 10 system recommendations covering construction scheduling, capability floors, amortization via query volume, freshness-latency tradeoffs, and fleet-scale management.

Original abstract: Sparse attention is becoming increasingly important for serving large language models (LLMs) as generation lengths continue to grow. To address this challenge, we present Vortex, a system that combines a Python-embedded frontend language atop a page-centric tensor abstraction for expressing a broad range of sparse attention algorithms, with an efficient backend tightly integrated into modern LLM serving stacks. Vortex enables rapid prototyping, deployment, and evaluation of sparse attention algorithms, effectively translating their theoretical efficiency gains into real-world throughput improvements. As a result, Vortex substantially accelerates the design and iteration of sparse attention algorithms. First, AI agents use Vortex to automatically generate and refine diverse algorithms, the best reaching up to $3.46\times$ higher throughput than full attention while preserving accuracy. Original abstract: Benchmarks are fundamental for evaluating and advancing LLMs and MLLMs by providing standardized and explicit measures of performance. To address these challenges, we introduce Benchmark Agent, a fully autonomous agentic system designed for benchmark building. ### [64] [Goedel-Architect: Streamlining Formal Theorem Proving with Blueprint Generation and Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06468v1)
*Jui-Hui Chung,Ziyang Cai,Zihao Li,Qishuo Yin,Rohit Agarwal,Simon Park,Rodrigo Porto,Narutatsu Ri,Ziran Yang,Shange Tang,Xingyu Dang,Hongzhou Lin,Mengdi Wang,Danqi Chen,Chi Jin,Liam H Fowl,Sanjeev Arora*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 定理证明agent，可迁移至自动代码验证与优化

TL;DR: Goedel-Architect是一个用于Lean 4的定理证明框架，通过生成和细化蓝图（依赖图），并行证明引理，并以失败驱动全局改进。在多个基准测试上达到顶尖性能，成本降低数百倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有递归分解方法可能导致低效的死循环，需要更高效的全局策略来形式化证明。

Method: 首先生成包含定义和引理依赖的蓝图（可选由自然语言引导），然后使用工具增强的Lean证明器并行证明每个引理，失败引理触发蓝图细化。

Result: 在MiniF2F-test上达到99.2% pass@1，PutnamBench上75.6% pass@1；自然语言引导后进一步提升至100%和88.8%，并在IMO、Putnam、USAMO上取得佳绩。

Conclusion: Goedel-Architect以极低成本实现了开源管道的最先进定理证明性能。

中文摘要：我们介绍了Goedel-Architect，一个专注于蓝图生成和细化的Lean 4形式定理证明的智能体框架。蓝图是一个定义和引理的依赖图，逐步构建到主定理。首先，Goedel-Architect生成一个由正式陈述的定义和引理以及声明的依赖关系组成的蓝图。该蓝图可选地由自然语言证明引导。然后，一个配备工具的Lean证明器组件使用相关依赖关系并行关闭每个开放引理节点。失败的引理反过来驱动全局蓝图的细化。这种策略与其他主流方法形成对比，后者使用递归引理分解，并可能低效地循环在死胡同策略上。使用开放权重的DeepSeek-V4-Flash (284B-A13B)作为骨干，Goedel-Architect在MiniF2F-test上达到99.2% pass@1，在PutnamBench上达到75.6% pass@1。可选地在较难问题上用自然语言证明播种初始蓝图，我们另外关闭了剩下的两个MiniF2F-test问题（达到100%），将PutnamBench提升到88.8% (597/672)，并在IMO 2025上解决了4/6，在Putnam 2025上解决了11/12，在USAMO 2026上解决了3/6。这代表了开源管道在最先进的性能，价格点比可比较的开源管道低高达500倍。

Original abstract: We introduce Goedel-Architect, an agentic framework for formal theorem proving in Lean 4 centered on blueprint generation and refinement. A blueprint is a dependency graph of definitions and lemmas that builds up to the main theorem. First, Goedel-Architect generates a blueprint of formally stated definitions and lemmas, along with declared dependencies. This blueprint is optionally guided by a natural language proof. Then, a tool-equipped Lean prover component closes each open lemma node in parallel using relevant dependencies. Failed lemmas in turn drive refinement of the global blueprint. This strategy contrasts with other mainstream approaches which use recursive lemma decomposition, and can inefficiently loop on dead-end strategies. Using the open-weight DeepSeek-V4-Flash (284B-A13B) as the backbone, Goedel-Architect attains 99.2% pass@1 on MiniF2F-test and 75.6% pass@1 on PutnamBench. With an optional natural-language proof seeding the initial blueprint on the harder problems, we additionally close the remaining two MiniF2F-test problems (reaching 100%), lift PutnamBench to 88.8% (597/672), and solve 4/6 on IMO 2025, 11/12 on Putnam 2025, and 3/6 on USAMO 2026. This represents state-of-the-art performance for an open-source pipeline at a price point up to 500x less than comparable open-source pipelines.

</details>

Method: 通过渐进式MCGS实现跨分支信息流和探索-利用平衡；引入回顾记忆结合冷启动知识库和动态全局内存；解耦战略规划与代码生成，采用自适应编码模式。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly applied to long-horizon tasks such as scientific discovery and machine learning engineering (MLE), where sustained self-evolution becomes a key capability. However, existing MLE agents suffer from inter-branch information isolation, memoryless search, and lack of hierarchical control, which together hinder long-horizon optimization. We present MLEvolve, an LLM-based self-evolving multi-agent framework for end-to-end machine learning algorithm discovery. By extending tree search to Progressive MCGS, MLEvolve enables cross-branch information flow through graph-based reference edges and gradually shifts the search from broad exploration to focused exploitation with an entropy-inspired progressive schedule. To allow the agent to evolve with accumulated experience, we introduce Retrospective Memory, which combines a cold-start domain knowledge base with a dynamic global memory for task-specific experience retrieval and reuse. For stable long-horizon iteration, we further decouple strategic planning from code generation with adaptive coding modes. Evaluation on MLE-Bench shows that MLEvolve achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple dimensions including average medal rate and valid submission rate under a 12-hour budget (half the standard runtime). Moreover, MLEvolve also outperforms specialized algorithm discovery methods including AlphaEvolve on mathematical algorithm optimization tasks, demonstrating strong cross-domain generalization. Our code is available at https://github.com/InternScience/MLEvolve.

### [66] [AEGIS: A Backup Reflex for Physical AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06660v1)
*Josef Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出AEGIS框架，通过轻量探针检测高风险步骤并切换强策略，是一种agent故障恢复与选择性控制方法，可迁移至coding agent的容错设计。

TL;DR: AEGIS通过在弱策略的冻结激活上使用轻量级探针检测高风险步骤，并在必要时切换到强策略，显著提高了长程机器人操作的恢复率，且仅增加少量计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程机器人操作容易因单步错误而逐渐失败，且失败前往往有预兆。现有方法要么在每一步都使用强策略（成本高），要么随机或盲目升级（效果差）。因此需要一种能准确预测高风险步骤并仅在必要时升级的方法。

Method: AEGIS包含一个轻量级探针，从弱策略的冻结激活中学习预测任务失败概率；当探针预测高风险时，将控制切换到强策略，否则由弱策略执行。探针仅在前30%的轨迹步骤上训练，使用AUROC作为评估指标。

Result: 在LIBERO-Spatial上，AEGIS恢复10.1%的失败轨迹，显著优于预算匹配的盲目升级（4.6%）和随机触发（5.1%）。探针的早期窗口AUROC为0.764，仅在38%的步骤激活强策略。

Conclusion: AEGIS通过精准的早期预警和选择性升级，证明了时机而非计算量是提升长程操作鲁棒性的关键，且该方法可预注册、可复现。

中文摘要：长程机器人操作往往逐渐失败：一个错误的步骤会降低状态，策略就会陷入无法恢复的困境。失败在发生前通常是可见的。我们提出了AEGIS（激活探针预警、门控推理切换），一种选择性升级方法，它使用一个轻量级探针在弱策略的冻结激活上检测高风险步骤，同时仍有时间采取行动。当探针标记一个步骤时，控制权切换到另一个更强的策略，但仅针对需要它的步骤。在LIBERO-Spatial上，AEGIS恢复了弱策略单独丢失的轨迹中的10.1%，而预算匹配的盲目升级为4.6%，随机触发安慰剂为5.1%。这些增益在带有Holm-Bonferroni调整的单侧精确配对McNemar检验下显著，针对三个预注册对比：比盲目升级高5.4个百分点，p=8.5e-6；比随机触发高5.0个百分点，p=1.0e-4；配对轨迹自举置信区间排除零。AEGIS仅在38%的步骤中激活强策略，因此杠杆是时机而非计算量。探针在早期窗口AUROC为0.764，95%置信区间[0.70, 0.84]（在第一次移交前从弱策略路径的前30%轨迹步骤读取）满足其前置条件。我们预注册了完整的分析计划，包括条件恢复任务率估计量和明确的终止标准，并在每个臂700个公共随机数回合上确认结果，nA_fail=646。

Original abstract: Long-horizon robot manipulation tends to fail gradually: one bad step degrades the state, and the policy spirals into a basin from which it cannot recover. The failure is often visible before it happens. We introduce AEGIS (Activation-probe Early-warning, Gated Inference Switching), a selective escalation method that uses a lightweight probe on a weak policy's frozen activations to detect high-risk steps while there is still time to act. When the probe flags a step, control switches to a stronger separate policy, but only for the steps that need it. On LIBERO-Spatial, AEGIS recovers 10.1% of the trajectories the weak policy alone loses, versus 4.6% for budget-matched blind escalation and 5.1% for a random-trigger placebo. These gains are significant under one-sided exact paired McNemar tests with Holm-Bonferroni adjustment over three pre-registered contrasts: +5.4pp over blind escalation, p=8.5e-6; +5.0pp over random triggering, p=1.0e-4; paired-trajectory bootstrap CIs exclude zero. AEGIS activates the stronger policy on only 38% of steps, so the lever is timing rather than compute. The probe clears its precondition with an early-window AUROC of 0.764, 95% CI [0.70, 0.84], read from the weak-policy path over the first 30% of trajectory steps before any handoff. We pre-register the full analysis plan, including a conditional recovered-task-rate estimand and explicit kill criteria, and confirm the result on 700 common-random-number episodes per arm, with nA-fail=646.

</details>


### [67] [OpenSkill: Open-World Self-Evolution for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06741v1)
*Zhiling Yan,Dingjie Song,Hanrong Zhang,Wei Liang,Yuxuan Zhang,Yutong Dai,Lifang He,Philip S. Yu,Ran Xu,Xiang Li,Lichao Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出OpenSkill框架，使LLM agent在无监督下从开放世界自行构建技能与验证信号并进行自我进化，直接对应agent的自我改进与技能学习研究。

TL;DR: OpenSkill框架使智能体在无目标任务监督下，通过利用开放世界资源自我构建技能和验证信号，实现自我进化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法假设存在可用学习循环（如精心策划的技能、成功轨迹或验证器信号），但真实开放世界部署仅提供任务提示，缺乏这些监督信号。

Method: 提出OpenSkill框架，从文档、代码库和网络中获取基础知识和验证锚点，合成可迁移技能，并通过基于锚点构建的虚拟任务进行自我完善。

Result: 在三个基准和两个目标智能体上，OpenSkill在无监督约束下取得了最佳自动化通过率，且技能可跨模型迁移，自建验证器与真实结果一致。

Conclusion: OpenSkill通过利用开放世界资源，实现了无需目标任务监督的自我进化，为开放世界智能体部署提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：自我进化智能体需要在部署后进行适应，但现有方法假设存在可用的学习循环，例如精心策划的技能、成功轨迹或验证器信号。真实的开放世界部署可能不提供这些，仅提供一个任务提示。在这项工作中，我们研究开放世界自我进化，其中智能体必须从零开始构建其技能和自身的验证信号，使用开放世界资源但没有目标任务监督。我们提出OpenSkill，一个引导此循环的框架：它从文档、代码库和网络中获取基础知识和验证锚点，将它们合成为可迁移的技能，并根据基于锚点而非目标答案的自我构建虚拟任务来完善这些技能。因此，开放世界既提供了要学习的知识，也提供了一个独立于监督的实践环境，目标任务监督保留用于最终评估。在三个基准和两个目标智能体上，OpenSkill在满足无监督约束的同时取得了最佳自动化通过率。分析表明，其技能无需模型特定适应即可跨模型迁移，且其自建验证器尽管从未访问真实结果，但与真实结果一致。

Original abstract: Self-evolving agents requires adaptation after deployment, but existing approaches assume a usable learning loop, such as curated skills, successful trajectories, or verifier signals. Real open-world deployments may provide none of these, offering only a task prompt. In this work, we study open-world self-evolution, where an agent must build both its skills and its own verification signals from scratch, using open-world resources but no target-task supervision. We propose OpenSkill, a framework that bootstraps this loop: it acquires grounded knowledge and verification anchors from documentation, repositories, and the web, synthesizes them into transferable skills, and refines those skills against self-built virtual tasks grounded in the anchors rather than in target answers. The open world thus supplies both the knowledge to be learned and a supervision-independent practice environment, with target-task supervision reserved for final evaluation. Across three benchmarks and two target agents, OpenSkill attains the best automated pass rate while satisfying the no-supervision constraint. Analysis shows its skills transfer across models without model-specific adaptation, and its self-built verifier aligns with ground-truth outcomes despite never accessing them.

</details>

### [68] [MPCoT: Reward-Guided Multi-Path Latent Reasoning for Test-Time Scalable Vision-Language-Action](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06245v1)
*Boyang Zhang,Lianlei Shan*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 多路径潜在推理框架用于VLA策略，属于通用agent推理规划方法。

TL;DR: 提出MPCOT，一种奖励引导的多路径潜在推理框架，通过多路径细化和软聚合提升VLA策略的长期性能，且不增加推理令牌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA策略在长期高不确定性任务中因一次性动作解码缺乏推理审慎性，而显式思维链引入令牌延迟和间接接口问题。

Method: MPCOT初始化M个潜在假设，经K步权重绑定细化后软聚合，通过训练阶段路径偏好目标（结合专家一致性、世界模型进展和成功反馈）优化路径评分器。

Result: 在LIBERO和CALVIN基准上，MPCOT显著提升长期任务成功率，消融实验证实深度宽度效应、置信度加权聚合和奖励引导监督的有效性。

Conclusion: MPCOT在保持8步动作接口和零推理令牌优势的同时，通过多路径潜在推理有效提升了VLA策略的长期控制性能。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略在长期和高不确定性控制中仍然脆弱，其中一次性动作解码提供的推理时间审慎性有限。显式的思维链可以增加推理深度，但引入了令牌延迟和间接的文本到动作接口。我们提出MPCOT，一种奖励引导的多路径潜在推理框架，该框架初始化M个假设，对它们进行K个权重绑定步骤的细化，并在动作解码前进行软聚合。仅限训练的路径偏好目标通过专家动作一致性、基于世界模型/VLM的进展和成功反馈来评估候选动作分支，以将潜在路径评分器与下游执行质量对齐。MPCOT保留了原始的8步动作接口，生成了零推理令牌，并暴露了可配置的推理控制（K,M）。在LIBERO和CALVIN上的匹配协议下，MPCOT提高了长期性能，消融实验确认了深度宽度效应、置信度加权聚合和奖励引导的路径监督。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies remain brittle in long-horizon and high-uncertainty control, where one-pass action decoding provides limited inference-time deliberation. Explicit chain-of-thought can increase reasoning depth, but introduces token latency and an indirect text-to-action interface. We propose MPCoT, a reward-guided multi-path latent reasoning framework that initializes $M$ hypotheses, refines them for K weight-tied steps, and softly aggregates them before action decoding. A training-only path-preference objective evaluates candidate action branches with expert-action consistency, world-model/VLM-based progress, and success feedback to align the latent path scorer with downstream execution quality. MPCoT preserves the original 8-step action interface, generates zero reasoning tokens, and exposes configurable inference controls (K,M). Under matched protocols on LIBERO and CALVIN, MPCoT improves long-horizon performance, with ablations confirming depth-width effects, confidence-weighted aggregation, and reward-guided path supervision.

</details>


### [69] [SCOUT: Semantic scene COverage via Uncertainty-guided Traversal](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06721v1)
*Junyu Mao,Sara Ayoubi,Vishnu D. Sharma,Ilija Hadžić,Matthew Andrews*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出SCOUT在线语义探索框架，耦合主动遍历与场景图构建，涉及不确定性引导的规划，对agent在复杂环境中的探索策略有启发。

TL;DR: SCOUT是一个在线语义探索框架，通过主动遍历与概率场景图构建闭环，使机器人能根据不确定性引导决策，逐步构建并维护语义完整的3D场景图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D场景图感知多作为固定数据集的离线后处理，无法与探索决策交互，限制了机器人在持续操作中对环境的主动理解。

Method: 提出SCOUT框架，结合不确定性感知的3D场景图构建与不确定性引导的遍历规划，通过平衡语义确定性增益、几何覆盖和移动成本选择视点，实现闭环主动探索。

Result: 机器人能够在线增量构建场景图，并根据信念不确定性重新访问模糊对象或扩展未知空间，提升语义完整性。

Conclusion: SCOUT将语义场景完整性作为操作目标，使机器人能在最小人工干预下自主巡逻和更新环境，迈向更主动的场景理解代理。

中文摘要：在长时间运行的机器人不应仅仅访问空间，而应逐步理解空间。然而，大多数3D场景图流水线将感知视为固定数据集上的后处理阶段，将场景表示与决定首先观察到什么的决策分离开来。我们提出了SCOUT，一种在线语义探索框架，通过将主动遍历与概率场景图构建相结合来闭环。给定先验的2D占用地图和带有姿态的RGB-D观测，SCOUT增量式地构建一个不确定性感知的3D场景图，其节点维护融合的几何形状和开放词汇对象标签的后验信念，而边则编码结构关系，如在上、内部、属于和旁边。这些信念被反馈给不确定性引导的遍历规划器，该规划器通过平衡期望的语义确定性增益、几何覆盖增益和移动成本来选择视点。这样，当额外证据重要时，机器人会重新访问模糊对象，当场景仍然不完整时，则会扩展到未知自由空间。由此产生的系统将语义场景完整性视为操作目标，而非语义映射的被动副产品，朝着能够在最少人工干预下巡逻、更新和推理演化中的室内环境的自主代理迈进。

Original abstract: Robots that operate over extended periods should not merely visit space; they should progressively understand it. Yet most 3D scene graph pipelines treat perception as a post-processing stage over a fixed dataset, decoupling scene representation from the decisions that determine what is observed in the first place. We present SCOUT, an online semantic exploration framework that closes this loop by coupling active traversal with probabilistic scene graph construction. Given a prior 2D occupancy map and posed RGB-D observations, SCOUT incrementally builds an uncertainty-aware 3D scene graph whose nodes maintain fused geometry and posterior beliefs over open-vocabulary object labels, while edges encode structural relations such as on, inside, belong, and next to. These beliefs are fed back to an uncertainty-guided traversal planner, which selects viewpoints by balancing expected semantic certainty gain, geometric coverage gain, and travel cost. In this way, the robot revisits ambiguous objects when additional evidence matters and expands into unseen free space when the scene remains incomplete. The resulting system treats semantic scene completeness as an operational objective rather than a passive by-product of semantic mapping, moving toward autonomous agents that can patrol, update, and reason about evolving indoor environments with minimal human intervention.

</details>

### [70] [Agent-Orchestrated Adaptive RAG: A Comparative Study on Structured and Multi-Hop Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05658v1)
*Anuj Maharjan,Devinder Kaur,Richard Molyet*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: Agent编排的Adaptive RAG框架，涉及动态规划与反思，通用agent方法

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于智能体编排的自适应RAG框架，通过动态查询分解和迭代检索提升性能，但实验表明这些增强并非普遍有益，需根据领域和查询特征选择性应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG依赖静态单步检索，在处理复杂查询时性能受限，需要更动态和自适应的检索策略。

Method: 提出Agent-Orchestrated Adaptive RAG框架，包含动态查询分解、迭代检索和有界自反思评估循环。

Result: 查询分解在结构化领域（DevOps）提升总体得分+0.04和MRR+0.17，但在多跳基准MuSiQue上降低排序精度；反思机制提高引文准确性但增加延迟。

Conclusion: 智能体增强应自适应、成本感知地选择，而非统一使用激进的推理流水线。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）通过将大语言模型（LLM）的响应锚定在外部知识上来增强其能力，但传统的流水线依赖于静态的单步检索，这限制了其在复杂查询上的性能。本文提出了一种基于智能体编排的自适应RAG框架，该框架引入了动态查询分解、迭代检索以及有界自反思评估循环。我们在两个互补的数据集上评估了该系统：一个特定领域的DevOps知识库和多跳推理基准MuSiQue。使用包括总体得分、引文准确性、平均倒数排名和主题覆盖度在内的指标，我们发现查询分解在结构化领域带来了一致的提升（在DevOps上总体得分+0.04，MRR+0.17），但在多跳基准上降低了排序精度，而反思机制以显著的延迟成本提高了引文准确性。这些对比结果表明，智能体增强并非普遍有益，必须根据查询和领域特征有选择地应用。我们的研究结果主张采用自适应、成本感知的编排，而不是统一激进的推理流水线。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances Large Language Models (LLMs) by grounding their responses in external knowledge, but conventional pipelines rely on static, single-step retrieval that limits performance on complex queries. This paper presents an Agent-Orchestrated Adaptive RAG framework that introduces dynamic query decomposition, iterative retrieval, and a bounded self-reflective evaluation loop. We evaluate the system across two complementary datasets: a domain-specific DevOps knowledge base and the multi-hop reasoning benchmark MuSiQue. Using metrics that include overall score, citation accuracy, mean reciprocal rank, and topic coverage, we find that query decomposition yields consistent gains in the structured domain (overall score $+0.04$, MRR $+0.17$ on DevOps) but degrades ranking precision on the multi-hop benchmark, while the reflection mechanism improves citation accuracy at a substantial latency cost. These contrasting results show that agentic enhancements are not universally beneficial and must be applied selectively according to query and domain characteristics. Our findings argue for adaptive, cost-aware orchestration rather than uniformly aggressive reasoning pipelines.
