### [71] [Cross-Epoch Adaptive Rollout Optimization for RL Post-Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05606v1)
*Yiming Zong,Yige Wang,Jiashuo Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自适应rollout分配方法用于LLM后训练，属于训练推理优化，对agent的样本效率提升有一般性启发。

TL;DR: 提出CERO方法，通过自适应分配展开预算提高LLM后训练样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对每个提示使用固定展开预算，忽略了不同提示提供训练信号的差异，导致样本效率低下。

Method: 将问题形式化为在线资源分配，维护Beta后验估计每个提示的成功概率，使用后验期望伯努利方差作为额外展开的价值，构建凹形饱和效用函数，并通过Fenchel对偶和投影在线梯度下降优化。

Result: 在数学推理任务中，CERO在多个LLM和基准上一致优于GRPO，实现了O(√K)遗憾界。

Conclusion: 自适应展开预算能够显著提高样本效率，CERO是有效的自适应分配方法。

中文摘要：大型语言模型的后训练通常依赖于强化学习方法，这些方法为每个提示采样多个展开（rollouts），但大多数现有方法对每个提示使用固定的展开预算，尽管不同提示提供的训练信号存在巨大差异。在本文中，我们研究了在固定全局预算下的自适应展开分配，并将该问题形式化为具有提示级边际收益递减的在线资源分配问题。我们的方法CERO维护每个提示成功概率的贝塔后验分布，并使用后验期望伯努利方差作为额外展开价值的贝叶斯估计。我们利用该估计构建了一个关于累积分配量的凹形饱和效用函数，得到了一个目标函数，其中跨提示和跨轮次的决策通过全局预算耦合。由于所得目标函数在时间上不可分离，我们推导了Fenchel对偶重构，并通过投影在线梯度下降更新提示级和预算级对偶变量。在固定提示效用下，我们证明了一个相对于离线分配基准的O(√K)遗憾界。在数学推理问题上的实验表明，CERO在多个开放权重的大型语言模型和基准测试中一致优于GRPO，证明了自适应展开预算能够提高样本效率。

Original abstract: LLM post-training often relies on reinforcement learning methods that sample multiple rollouts per prompt, yet most existing approaches use a fixed rollout budget for every prompt, despite large differences in the training signal different prompts provide. In this paper, we study adaptive rollout allocation under a fixed global budget and formulate the problem as online resource allocation with prompt-level diminishing returns. Our method, CERO, maintains a Beta posterior over each prompt's success probability and uses the posterior expected Bernoulli variance as a Bayesian estimate of the value of additional rollouts. We use this estimate to construct a concave, saturating utility over cumulative allocations, yielding an objective in which decisions across prompts and epochs are coupled by the global budget. Since the resulting objective is temporally nonseparable, we derive a Fenchel-dual reformulation and update both prompt-level and budget-level dual variables via projected online gradient descent. Under fixed prompt utilities, we prove an $O(\sqrt{K})$ regret bound against the offline allocation benchmark. Experiments on mathematical-reasoning problems show that CERO consistently outperforms GRPO across multiple open-weight LLMs and benchmarks, demonstrating that adaptive rollout budgeting can improve sample efficiency.

</details>


### [72] [MDP-GRPO: Stabilized Group Relative Policy Optimization for Multi-Constraint Instruction Following](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06058v1)
*Mohammad Mahdi Salmani-Zarchi,Zahra Rahimi,Heshaam Faili,Mohammad Javad Dousti*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出稳定GRPO的方法，适用于多约束指令跟随agent训练。

TL;DR: 提出MDP-GRPO，通过多温度采样、双锚优势、前景理论塑形和非对称KL正则化，解决了标准GRPO在离散低分散奖励下的不稳定性，在多个约束跟随任务上提升严格约束满足率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准GRPO在离散、低分散奖励下不稳定，因为组内奖励分布常同质，导致低方差放大、均值中心盲目和零方差崩溃三种病理。

Method: 采用多温度采样增加奖励分散度，双锚优势在均匀组中恢复梯度，前景理论塑形限制更新并惩罚违规，以及非对称KL正则化稳定学习。

Result: 在FollowBench、IFEval和自建多约束数据集上，MDP-GRPO在Llama-3.2-3B上严格约束满足率提升高达5.0%，且小批量组尺寸下稳定收敛，保持MMLU和ARC上的通用能力。

Conclusion: MDP-GRPO有效解决了GRPO在低分散奖励下的不稳定性，显著提升多约束指令跟随性能，同时保证通用能力。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习是多约束指令跟随的理想选择，然而标准的组相对策略优化（GRPO）在离散、低分散奖励下变得不稳定，因为组内奖励分布通常同质。我们识别并形式化了在这种情况下的z-score组归一化的三种病理：低方差放大、均值中心盲目和零方差崩溃。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了MDP-GRPO，它通过以下方式稳定学习：(1) 多温度采样以增加奖励分散度，(2) 双锚优势以在均匀组中恢复梯度并停止均值中心盲目，(3) 前景理论塑形以基于卡尼曼和特沃斯基的理论限制更新并惩罚违规，(4) 非对称KL正则化。在FollowBench、IFEval和精心策划的多约束数据集上的评估表明，MDP-GRPO优于标准GRPO，在Llama-3.2-3B上严格约束满足率提升高达5.0%。我们的方法还在小批量组尺寸下实现稳定收敛，同时保持MMLU和ARC上的通用能力。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is ideal for multi-constraint instruction following, yet standard group-relative policy optimization (GRPO) becomes unstable under discrete, low-dispersion rewards, where within-group reward distributions are frequently homogeneous. We identify and formalize three pathologies of z-score group normalization in this regime: low-variance amplification, mean-centering blindness, and zero-variance collapse. To address them, we propose MDP-GRPO, which stabilizes learning through (1) multi-temperature sampling to increase reward dispersion, (2) dual-anchor advantages to restore gradients in homogeneous groups and stop mean-centering blindness, (3) prospect-theoretic shaping to bound updates and penalize violations based on Kahneman and Tversky's theory, and (4) asymmetric KL regularization. Evaluated on FollowBench, IFEval, and a curated multi-constraint dataset, MDP-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO, improving strict constraint satisfaction by up to 5.0% on Llama-3.2-3B. Our method also enables stable convergence with small group sizes while preserving general capabilities on MMLU and ARC.

</details>


### [73] [Learning to Route LLMs from Implicit Cost-Performance Preferences via Meta-Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06178v1)
*Jiahao Zeng,Ming Tang,Ningning Ding*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出元学习框架路由LLM以优化成本-性能，对agent中的模型选择与资源管理有启发。

TL;DR: 提出MetaRouter，一种基于元学习的LLM路由框架，通过少量交互学习用户隐式偏好，实现个性化成本-性能优化，在多种任务上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM路由方法无法适应不同用户对成本-性能的偏好，需要一种能够高效学习用户隐式偏好并个性化优化的方法。

Method: 将用户偏好配置为上下文赌博机中的不同任务，提出基于元学习的MetaRouter框架，通过少量交互学习用户隐式偏好并实现偏好感知的路由决策。

Result: MetaRouter在分布内和分布外任务上均优于强基线，学习用户偏好高效，对可路由LLM变化鲁棒，并支持多模型路由扩展。

Conclusion: MetaRouter有效解决了LLM路由中用户偏好异质性问题，实现了个性化成本-性能优化，具有高效、鲁棒和可扩展的优点。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在性能与成本之间呈现权衡，更强大的模型会带来更高的费用。LLM路由旨在通过在查询时选择最合适的模型来降低成本同时保持性能。然而，现有方法无法很好地适应不同用户对成本-性能的偏好。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了一种新颖的感知性LLM路由范式，用于个性化和以用户为中心的成本-性能优化，通过少量交互高效地学习用户的隐式偏好。为了处理异构用户需求的挑战，我们将偏好配置表述为上下文赌博机中的一组不同任务，并提出了MetaRouter，一个用于偏好感知LLM路由的元学习框架。实验结果表明，MetaRouter在分布内和分布外任务上都优于强基线。此外，它在学习用户偏好方面表现出高效率，对可路由LLM的变化具有鲁棒性，并且可扩展到多模型路由。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) present a trade-off between performance and cost, where more powerful models incur greater expense. LLM routing aims to mitigate expenses while maintaining performance by sending queries to the most suitable model. However, existing methods cannot perform well for different user cost-performance preferences. To address this gap, we introduce a novel perceptive LLM routing paradigm for personalized and user-centric cost-performance optimization, which efficiently learns users' implicit preferences through little interaction. To handle the challenge of heterogeneous user needs, we formulate preference profiles as a set of distinct tasks in contextual bandit and propose MetaRouter, a meta-learning framework designed for preference-aware LLM routing. Experimental results show that MetaRouter outperforms strong baselines on both in-distribution and out-of-distribution tasks. Furthermore, it exhibits high efficiency in learning user preferences, robustness to changes in the routable LLMs, and scalability to multi-model routing.

### [74] [MacArena: Benchmarking Computer Use Agents on an Online macOS Environment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06560v1)
*Victor Muryn,Maksym Shamrai,Sofiia Mazepa,Yehor Khodysko*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 构建macOS计算机使用agent基准，直接相关GUI agent评估，对coding agent有参考。

TL;DR: MacArena是一个针对macOS的GUI代理基准，包含421个任务，发现现有模型在macOS上性能显著下降，表明跨平台GUI能力不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: macOS缺乏全面的GUI代理基准，现有基准覆盖不全且不兼容Apple Silicon，无法评估真实跨平台能力。

Method: 构建MacArena基准，整合OSWorld和macOSWorld的移植任务及49个新macOS原生任务，共421个任务，在Apple Silicon上通过原生虚拟化框架运行。

Result: 模型在移植任务和macOS原生任务间排名反转，领先模型在MacArena子集上落后超过26%。

Conclusion: macOS对GUI代理更具挑战性，现有基准不能反映真正的跨平台能力，模型表现受任务分布熟悉度影响。

中文摘要：计算机使用代理（CUA）通过视觉和控制原语操作图形用户界面（GUI），其能力迅速发展，部分得益于标准化的在线评估基准如OSWorld，这些基准既作为评估工具，也作为强化学习的训练环境。然而，macOS在这一领域仍未被充分服务：现有的唯一基准macOSWorld仅覆盖了少量第一方应用程序，任务较为简单，且运行在与Apple Silicon不兼容的x86虚拟机上。我们引入了MacArena，一个包含421个手工验证任务、覆盖50个应用程序的基准，它结合了OSWorld任务的精选移植、来自macOSWorld的内容以及49个新的macOS原生任务，所有这些都运行在Apple Silicon上的Apple原生虚拟化框架上。我们认为macOS提出了Linux基准无法捕捉的独特GUI挑战，我们的评估支持这一观点：模型在现有基准上的强表现可能反映的是对任务分布的熟悉，而非真正的跨平台GUI能力。值得注意的是，在移植任务和macOS原生任务之间，模型排名发生反转，一个领先模型在MacArena子集上落后超过26%，这表明macOS对当前的GUI代理构成了一个真正更困难的环境。

Original abstract: Computer-use agents (CUAs) operate graphical user interfaces (GUIs) through vision and control primitives, and their capabilities have advanced rapidly, driven in part by standardized online evaluation benchmarks such as OSWorld, which serve both as evaluation tools and as training environments for reinforcement learning. However, macOS remains underserved in this landscape: the only existing benchmark, macOSWorld, covers a narrow slice of first-party applications with simpler tasks, and runs on x86 virtual machines incompatible with Apple Silicon. We introduce MacArena, a benchmark of 421 manually verified tasks spanning 50 applications that combines a curated port of OSWorld tasks, content sourced from macOSWorld, and 49 new macOS-native tasks, all running on Apple's native Virtualization framework on Apple Silicon. We argue that macOS presents distinct GUI challenges beyond what Linux-based benchmarks capture, and our evaluation supports this claim: strong model performance on existing benchmarks can reflect familiarity with task distributions rather than genuine cross-platform GUI competence. Notably, model rankings invert between ported and macOS-native tasks, with a leading model trailing by over 26% on the MacArena subset, suggesting that macOS poses a genuinely harder environment for current GUI agents.

### [75] [Tangram: Unlocking Non-Uniform KV Cache Compression for Efficient Multi-turn LLM Serving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06302v2)
*Hyungmin Kim,Minsoo Kim,Hongseok Kim,Jungwook Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Tangram通过静态预算预留、参差不齐分页和提前负载均衡，解决了非均匀KV压缩在LLM服务中的内存碎片和负载不平衡问题，实现了高达2.6倍的吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮LLM服务中KV缓存快速增长使得内存成为瓶颈，非均匀KV压缩虽精度高但导致页面碎片、预填充延迟和GPU负载不平衡，现有动态处理方法开销大。

Method: 基于离线校准的头保留结构规律，Tangram采用预算预留固定头压缩后大小、参差不齐分页聚类相似预算头、提前负载均衡预计算GPU分区，静态解决动态问题。

Result: 在vLLM上实现，匹配现有非均匀压缩精度，端到端吞吐量相比完整KV基线提升高达2.6倍。

Conclusion: Tangram通过静态优化实现了非均匀KV压缩的高效部署，显著提升LLM服务吞吐量，且易于集成现有方法。

中文摘要：多轮LLM服务会累积对话历史，其键值（KV）缓存随着每一轮和每个用户而增长，迅速超过模型权重本身，使得内存（而非计算）成为吞吐量的约束瓶颈。非均匀KV压缩在不同注意力头之间分配异构预算，其精度远优于均匀方案，但仍不实用：现代服务栈假设各头的KV长度相同，因此异构性会使释放的内存以页面碎片形式存在，在预填充阶段花费高达25%的时间回收分散的页面，并使GPU工作负载不均衡，导致解码延迟增加多达1.7倍，或在每个解码步骤中浪费15-20%的时间进行重新规划。我们观察到这种异构性无需在运行时发现：逐头的保留遵循两级结构规律——输入无关的头排名以及狭窄有界的逐头比例——这些可以从少至50个样本中离线校准。基于这一见解，我们提出了Tangram，一个服务框架，它静态地解决了先前系统动态处理的问题：预算预留（Budget Reservation）在调度时固定每个头压缩后的足迹，消除了页面回收；参差不齐分页（Ragged Paging）将相似预算的头聚类为独立的页表，将碎片转化为可回收内存；以及提前负载均衡（Ahead-of-Time Load Balancing）预计算均衡的GPU分区，无需运行时规划。在vLLM上实现的Tangram作为现有非均匀压缩方法的即插即用基础，在匹配其精度的同时，将端到端吞吐量相对于完整KV基线提升了多达2.6倍。我们的实现已在https://github.com/aiha-lab/TANGRAM公开。

Original abstract: Multi-turn LLM serving accumulates dialogue history whose Key-Value (KV) cache grows with every turn and every user, quickly exceeding the model weights themselves and making memory -- not compute -- the binding constraint on throughput. Non-uniform KV compression, which allocates heterogeneous budgets across attention heads, preserves accuracy far better than uniform schemes, yet remains impractical: modern serving stacks assume identical KV lengths across heads, so heterogeneity traps freed memory as page fragmentation, spends up to 25% of prefill time reclaiming scattered pages, and skews GPU workloads that inflate decode latency by up to $1.7\times$ or burn 15--20% of each decode step on re-planning. We observe that this heterogeneity need not be discovered at runtime: head-wise retention follows a two-level structural regularity -- an input-invariant head ranking with narrowly bounded per-head ratios -- that can be calibrated offline from as few as 50 samples. Building on this insight, we present Tangram, a serving framework that statically resolves what prior systems handle dynamically: Budget Reservation fixes each head's post-compression footprint at scheduling time, eliminating page reclamation; Ragged Paging clusters similar-budget heads into independent page tables, turning fragmentation into reclaimable memory; and Ahead-of-Time Load Balancing precomputes balanced GPU partitions with zero runtime planning. Implemented on vLLM, Tangram serves as a drop-in substrate for existing non-uniform compression methods, matching their accuracy while improving end-to-end throughput by up to $2.6\times$ over the full-KV baseline. Our implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/aiha-lab/TANGRAM.

</details>

### [76] [TensorBench: Benchmarking Coding Agents on a Compiler-Based Tensor Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05570v1)
*Bobby Yan,Fredrik Kjolstad*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 直接相关：在编译器张量框架上评估coding agent的代码添加和重构任务，涉及代码效率和自动化优化。

TL;DR: TensorBench是一个包含199个编码任务的基准测试，用于评估编码智能体，通过自动测试套件评分，发现最强智能体通过率64.8%，最弱22.1%，且智能体间一致性低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有存储库级别编码基准在任务难度和评估可靠性之间存在权衡，需要一种可扩展且可靠的自动化评估方法。

Method: 提出了TensorBench基准，包含199个功能添加和重构任务，通过应用智能体补丁并运行测试套件（包含现有测试和智能体添加的测试）自动评分，通过标准为保留原有行为并满足新功能检查。

Result: 评估了七个编码智能体，通过率范围64.8%至22.1%，智能体间任务通过子集差异大，Cohen's κ范围-0.07至0.43，最强两智能体κ=0.05。

Conclusion: TensorBench提供了可靠的自动化评估基准，揭示了当前编码智能体在复杂任务上表现差异显著且一致性低。

中文摘要：存储库级别的编码基准在任务难度和评估可靠性之间存在权衡：挑战前沿模型的任务通常涉及大型代码库且测试覆盖率不完整，而人工审查难以扩展。我们引入了TensorBench，这是一个包含199个功能添加和重构任务的基准测试，基于一个开源编译器驱动的张量框架，该框架扩展了PyTorch，为稠密和稀疏张量提供一流支持。任务涵盖新的稀疏格式、稠密优化过程、IR转换、调度器变更、运行时组件以及高级数值运算符。TensorBench通过应用智能体的补丁并运行框架的测试套件（包括预先存在的随机回归测试和智能体添加的任何测试）来对每次运行进行评分。对于功能添加任务，通过意味着修补后的代码库保留了经过测试的预先存在的行为，并满足智能体添加的针对请求功能的检查。我们评估了七个编码智能体，涵盖三个前沿模型家族和一个开放权重模型。在此标准下的通过率从最强智能体的64.8%到最弱智能体的22.1%不等。智能体通过了不同的任务子集：两两之间的Cohen's κ范围从-0.07到0.43，其中两个最强智能体的κ=0.05。

Original abstract: Repository-level coding benchmarks face a trade-off between task difficulty and evaluation reliability: tasks that challenge frontier models often involve large codebases with incomplete test coverage, while human review does not scale. We introduce TensorBench, a benchmark of 199 feature-addition and refactoring tasks on an open-source compiler-based tensor framework that extends PyTorch with first-class support for dense and sparse tensors. Tasks cover new sparse formats, dense optimization passes, IR transformations, scheduler changes, runtime components, and high-level numerical operators. TensorBench grades each run by applying the agent's patch and running the framework's test suite, which includes the pre-existing randomized regression tests and any tests the agent adds. For feature-addition tasks, a pass means that the patched repository preserves the tested pre-existing behavior and satisfies the agent-added checks for the requested feature. We evaluate seven coding agents spanning three frontier model families and one open-weight model. Pass rates under this criterion range from $64.8\%$ for the strongest agent to $22.1\%$ for the weakest. Agents pass different subsets of tasks: pairwise Cohen's $κ$ ranges from $-0.07$ to $0.43$, with $κ= 0.05$ for the two strongest agents.

</details>


### [77] [MARDoc: A Memory-Aware Refinement Agent Framework for Multimodal Long Document QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05749v1)
*Kaifeng Chen,Hongtao Liu,Qiyao Peng,Jian Yang,Yongqiang Liu,Xiaochen Zhang,Qing Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent记忆检索框架用于文档QA，可迁移至长代码agent

TL;DR: MARDoc通过三个解耦的智能体（探索者、精炼者、反射者）和结构化记忆，减少了多模态长文档问答中的上下文噪声，显著提升了多跳推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有迭代检索-推理系统混淆了检索轨迹、观察和推理，导致关键证据分散，多跳推理效果差。

Method: 将长文档问答分解为三个专门智能体：Explorer进行多粒度检索，Refiner提炼交互为结构化记忆，Reflector检查证据充分性并提供反馈；智能体依赖动态更新的结构化记忆而非完整历史。

Result: 在MMLongBench-Doc和DocBench上，MARDoc超越了同骨干基线，证明了结构化记忆的有效性。

Conclusion: 结构化记忆能有效减少上下文噪声，保留关键事实和逻辑依赖，提升智能体文档问答的性能。

中文摘要：迭代式的检索-推理智能体近期在多模态长文档问答中展现出潜力。然而，大多数现有系统维护一个持续增长的上下文，其中混合了检索轨迹、观察和中间推理。随着交互的累积，关键证据变得分散和稀释，使得多跳推理变得嘈杂。我们提出了MARDoc，一个内存感知的精炼智能体框架，将长文档问答解耦为三个专门的智能体：一个用于多粒度多模态检索的探索者，一个用于将交互轨迹提炼为结构化证据和推理记忆的精炼者，以及一个用于检查证据充分性并提供针对性反馈的反射者。在迭代过程中，智能体依赖动态更新的结构化记忆，而不是完整的累积交互历史。这种设计减少了上下文噪声，同时保留了答案关键事实及其逻辑依赖。在MMLongBench-Doc和DocBench上的实验表明，MARDoc取得了强劲的结果，优于同骨干基线，并证明了结构化记忆在智能体文档问答中的有效性。

Original abstract: Iterative retrieval-reasoning agents have recently shown promise for multimodal long-document question answering. However, most existing systems maintain a single growing context that mixes retrieval traces, observations, and intermediate reasoning. As interactions accumulate, key evidence becomes scattered and diluted, making multi-hop reasoning noisy. We propose MARDoc, a Memory-Aware Refinement Agent framework that decouples long-document QA into three specialized agents: an Explorer for multi-granularity multimodal retrieval, a Refiner for distilling interaction traces into structured evidence and reasoning memories, and a Reflector for checking evidence sufficiency and providing targeted feedback. Across iterations, the agents rely on a dynamically updated structured memory rather than a full accumulated interaction history. This design reduces context noise while preserving answer-critical facts and their logical dependencies. Experiments on MMLongBench-Doc and DocBench show that MARDoc achieves strong results, outperforming same-backbone baselines and demonstrating the effectiveness of structured memory for agentic document QA.

</details>


### [78] [CollabBench: Benchmarking and Unleashing Collaborative Ability of LLMs with Diverse Players via Proactive Engagement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05793v1)
*Hong Qian,Yuanhao Liu,Zihan Zhou,Zongbao Zhang,Hanjie Ge,Haotian Shi,Liang Dou,Xiangfeng Wang,Jingwen Yang,Aimin Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多智能体协作benchmark与训练范式，对agent合作研究有借鉴

TL;DR: CollabBench是一个在合作游戏中评估和训练协作LLM智能体的基准，通过多样化玩家模拟和混合奖励优化，实现了19.5%效率提升和24.4%情感改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话级协作研究缺乏基于互动的行为和实际执行，需要能够支持情境化和沉浸式协作的合作游戏环境。

Method: 提出CollabBench基准，包括多样化玩家档案模拟管道和协作智能体训练范式，该范式通过智能体回滚统一推理、沟通和行动，并使用混合奖励平衡任务效率和情感适应。扩展经典环境以支持多玩家个性化评估。

Result: 训练模型在效率和情感指标上分别超出基础模型19.5%和24.4%；分析揭示了现有模型的协作局限性。

Conclusion: CollabBench有效评估和训练协作智能体，提升协作性能，并为未来协作训练提供方向。

中文摘要：尽管基于LLM的智能体在个体任务上表现出色，但与真实人类伙伴的有效协作仍然具有挑战性。现有的大多数对话级协作研究缺乏基于互动的行为和实际执行，这激发了对能够实现情境化和沉浸式协作的合作游戏环境的需求。为此，本文提出了CollabBench，这是一个用于在合作游戏中评估和训练协作智能体的基准。CollabBench具有一个多样化的玩家档案模拟管道，用于建模不同的玩家行为，以及一个统一的协作智能体训练范式，该范式通过智能体回滚统一推理、沟通和行动，并通过平衡任务效率和情感适应的混合奖励进行优化。我们进一步将经典环境扩展到CWAH-MultiPlayer和Cook-MultiPlayer，以在多样化个性下进行系统评估。效率和情感度量的实验表明，我们训练的模型优于基础模型，实现了19.5%的效率提升和24.4%的情感表现改进。进一步分析揭示了现有模型的关键协作局限性，并为未来的协作训练提供了见解。

Original abstract: While LLM-based agents excel at individual tasks, effective collaboration with realistic human partners remains challenging. Most of the existing conversation-level collaborative studies lack grounded interaction and behavioral execution, motivating the need for cooperative game environments that enable contextualized and immersive collaboration. To this end, this paper proposes CollabBench, a benchmark for evaluating and training collaborative agents in cooperative games. CollabBench features a Diverse Player Profile Simulation pipeline to model varied players behaviors, and a Collaborative Agentic Training paradigm that unifies reasoning, communication, and action via agentic rollouts, optimized with a hybrid reward balancing task efficiency and affective adaptation. We further extend classic environments to CWAH-MultiPlayer and Cook-MultiPlayer for systematic evaluation under diverse personalities. Experiments with efficiency and affective metrics show that our trained models outperform base models, achieving 19.5% higher efficiency and 24.4% improved affective performance. Further analysis reveals key collaborative limitations of existing models and offers insights for future collaborative training.

</details>


### [79] [Reducing Hallucinations in Complex Question Answering using Simple Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (long version)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05901v1)
*Christopher J. Wedge,Joshua Stutter,Danny Dixon,Jacek Cała*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 图基RAG agent系统，涉及工具使用与检索，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 使用轻量级图结构增强RAG系统，显著提高事实正确性并减少幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM和RAG系统存在幻觉和无法处理专有信息的问题，而现有方法依赖昂贵微调，因此探索轻量图结构支持RAG。

Method: 设计智能体系统，集成向量搜索和图查询工具，基于维基百科结构化数据，在MoNaCo基准上评估。

Result: 图工具引入显著提升精确率和召回率，幻觉减半，细粒度真实性得分最高，令牌使用增加适度。

Conclusion: 轻量图结构有效增强RAG，提升事实正确性且成本低。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）从根本上改变了自然语言处理的面貌。尽管取得了这些进展，但LLM和基于LLM的系统仍然容易出现各种故障模式。检索增强生成（RAG）系统已成为一种常见的部署场景，旨在避免众所周知的LLM“幻觉”信息的风险，并能够在不诉诸昂贵的模型微调的情况下，对训练期间LLM无法访问的专有信息进行推理和问答。在这项工作中，我们探索了使用轻量级图结构和相对简单的图模式，通过专用工具集支持RAG子系统的想法。我们设计了一个智能体系统，该系统配备多种向量搜索和图查询工具，基于一个由精选的英文维基百科子集构成的结构化数据集，对来自MoNaCo（一个具有挑战性的维基百科问答基准，涉及复杂查询回答任务）的问题进行了评估。我们的结果表明，引入基于图的工具可以显著提高事实正确性的精确率和召回率，将幻觉答案的数量减半，并在三个评估场景中实现了最高的细粒度真实性得分。所有这一切仅以适度的令牌使用增加为代价。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have fundamentally transformed the landscape of Natural Language Processing. Despite these advances, LLMs and LLM-based systems remain prone to a variety of failure modes. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems have emerged as a common deployment scenario seeking to both avoid the well known risk of the LLM "hallucinating" information, and to enable reasoning and question answering over proprietary information that the LLM did not have access to during training without resorting to expensive model fine-tuning.
  In this work, we explore the idea of using a lightweight graph structure with a relatively simple graph schema, to support the RAG subsystem via a dedicated toolset. We design an agentic system with a variety of vector search and graph query tools operating over a structured dataset based on a curated subset of English Wikipedia articles, and evaluate its performance on questions from MoNaCo, a challenging Wikipedia QA benchmark of complex query answering tasks.
  Our results show that the introduction of graph-based tools can significantly increase the precision and recall of factual correctness, can halve the number of hallucinated answers, and achieves the highest fine-grained truthfulness score among the three evaluated scenarios. All this with a modest increase in token usage.

</details>


### [80] [LatentSkill: From In-Context Textual Skills to In-Weight Latent Skills for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06087v1)
*Aofan Yu,Chenyu Zhou,Tianyi Xu,Zihan Guo,Rong Shan,Zhihui Fu,Jun Wang,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang,Jianghao Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出将文本技能转换为LoRA适配器，减少上下文开销，对agent技能模块化与效率有启发。

TL;DR: 提出LatentSkill，通过超网络将文本技能转换为LoRA适配器，去除上下文中的技能令牌，在ALFWorld和Search-QA上提升性能并大幅降低开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能注入方式带来上下文开销和明文暴露问题，需要更高效且隐蔽的技能存储方法。

Method: 通过预训练超网络将文本技能转换为LoRA适配器，存储在权重空间中，实现即插即用、模块化加载、缩放和组合。

Result: 在ALFWorld上，seen和unseen分割成功率分别提升21.4和13.4个百分点，预填充令牌减少64.1%；在Search-QA上，精确匹配提升3.0个百分点，技能令牌开销降低72.2%。

Conclusion: 权重空间技能为LLM代理提供高效、模块化且暴露程度低的扩展基板，具有结构化语义几何和可组合性。

中文摘要：Agent系统越来越频繁地使用文本技能来编码可复用的任务流程，但在每一步都将这些技能注入提示中会带来大量的上下文开销，并将技能内容以明文形式暴露。我们提出了LatentSkill，这是一个通过预训练超网络将文本技能转换为即插即用LoRA适配器的框架。LatentSkill将技能知识存储在权重空间而非上下文空间，去除了每步技能令牌，同时保留了模块化加载、缩放和组合的能力。在ALFWorld和Search-QA上，LatentSkill优于相应的上下文技能基线，同时使用了更少的预填充令牌：在seen和unseen分割上，LatentSkill分别提升了21.4和13.4个百分点的成功率，且预填充令牌减少了64.1%；在Search-QA上，精确匹配提升了3.0个百分点，技能令牌开销降低了72.2%。进一步分析表明，生成的技能LoRA形成了结构化的语义几何形状，可以通过LoRA缩放系数精确控制，并且当技能组件对齐时可以通过参数空间算术进行组合。这些发现表明，权重空间技能为扩展LLM代理提供了一种高效、模块化且暴露程度更低的基板。

Original abstract: Agent systems increasingly use textual skills to encode reusable task procedures, but injecting these skills into the prompt at every step incurs substantial context overhead and exposes skill content as plaintext. We present LatentSkill, a framework that converts textual skills into plug-and-play LoRA adapters through a pretrained hypernetwork. LatentSkill stores skill knowledge in weight space rather than context space, removing per-step skill tokens while preserving modular loading, scaling, and composition. On ALFWorld and Search-QA, LatentSkill outperforms the corresponding in-context skill baseline while using substantially fewer prefill tokens: it improves ALFWorld success by 21.4 and 13.4 points on the seen and unseen splits with 64.1% fewer prefill tokens, and improves Search-QA exact match by 3.0 points with 72.2% lower skill-token overhead. Further analysis shows that generated skill LoRAs form a structured semantic geometry, can be precisely controlled via the LoRA scaling coefficient, and can be composed through parameter-space arithmetic when skill components are aligned. These findings suggest that weight-space skills provide an efficient, modular, and less exposed substrate for extending LLM agents.

</details>


### [81] [Dense Contexts Are Hard Contexts: Lexical Density Limits Effective Context in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06203v1)
*Giovanni Dettori,Matteo Boffa,Danilo Giordano,Idilio Drago,Marco Mellia*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 发现词汇密度影响LLM长上下文性能，对agent处理密集信息有实际启示。

TL;DR: 词汇密度是影响LLM长上下文性能的第三个关键因素，高密度导致有效上下文窗口缩小，降低密度可恢复性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注输入长度和相关信息位置对长上下文性能的影响，但忽略了信息密度这一因素，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 使用三个长度相同（～12k tokens）但信息密度递增的“找针”式基准，控制针位置，测试不同大小（9B-685B）的开源LLM，并通过在基准内改变密度来排除任务类型干扰。

Result: 高密度基准上模型性能急剧下降，从接近完美降至低于60%检索分数；降低密度可显著恢复性能，尤其是在高密度区域。

Conclusion: 有效上下文容量是词汇密度的函数，处理紧凑信息输入时需考虑密度因素，这对真实世界LLM系统有重要启示。

中文摘要：输入长度和相关信息的位置被广泛引为导致LLM长上下文性能下降的主要原因。本文研究词汇密度——上下文引入不同信息的速率——作为第三个被广泛忽视的因素，它系统地降低了LLM的有效上下文窗口。我们使用三个“找针”式基准测试（长度相同，约12k tokens，针位置受控，但信息密度递增）来量化词汇密度对开放权重LLM（9B-685B）的影响。我们观察到在高密度基准中性能急剧下降：在稀疏上下文中接近完美的模型，在密集上下文中检索分数降至60%以下。为排除任务类型干扰，我们在每个基准内改变并控制密度，同时保持其他所有属性不变。降低密度通常能恢复性能，尤其是在出现退化的高密度区域。这些结果表明，有效上下文容量是词汇密度的函数，这对处理紧凑、信息丰富输入的真实世界LLM系统有直接影响。

Original abstract: Input length and the position of relevant information are widely cited as the primary causes of degraded LLM long-context performance. Here, we study lexical density -- the rate at which a context introduces distinct information -- as a third, largely overlooked factor that systematically reduces the effective context window of LLMs. We quantify the impact of lexical density on open-weight LLMs (9B-685B) using three "find-the-needle" style benchmarks with identical length (~12k tokens) and controlled needle position, but increasing density of information. We observe a sharp performance collapse in higher-density benchmarks: models that are near-perfect in sparse contexts drop below 60% retrieval score on denser ones. To rule out task-type confounds, we vary and control the density within each benchmark while keeping all other properties unchanged. Reducing density generally restores performance, especially in the high-density regimes where degradation appears. These results show that effective context capacity is a function of lexical density, with direct implications for real-world LLM systems operating on compact, information-rich inputs.

</details>


### [82] [Human Adults and LLMs as Scientists: Who Benefits from Active Exploration?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06464v1)
*Mandana Samiei,Eunice Yiu,Anthony GX-Chen,Dongyan Lin,Jocelyn Shen,Blake A. Richards,Alison Gopnik,Doina Precup*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究LLM agent主动探索策略，对coding agent规划与探索有启发

TL;DR: 主动探索显著改善了成人的合取因果推理，但合取规则仍比析取规则更难；大型语言模型在推理准确性上接近人类，但探索策略效率较低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究显示成人有“合取障碍”，但多基于被动观察，本文探究主动探索能否克服此偏差。

Method: 使用改进的blicket探测器任务，让成人自由干预识别合取或析取规则下的因果对象，并与多个大型语言模型对比。

Result: 主动探索显著提升合取推理，但合取规则仍需更多测试；部分语言模型推理准确性接近人类，但探索效率较低且存在类似表现差距。

Conclusion: 主动探索有助于缓解合取障碍，但合取规则仍更具挑战；语言模型在推理上接近人类，但在探索策略上不如。

中文摘要：因果学习文献中的一个长期发现是，成人在识别合取因果规则（即效果需要多个原因同时存在）时存在困难，而在析取情境中表现更好。然而，大多数关于这种“合取障碍”的演示都依赖于被动观察范式，其中的证据有限，学习者无法控制证据的生成。本文探讨当成人通过主动探索获得自主性时，这种偏差是否仍然存在。使用改进的“blicket探测器”任务，成人参与者自由干预以识别合取或析取规则结构下的因果对象。我们表明，主动探索显著改善了成人的合取因果推理，尽管合取规则仍然需要比析取规则更多的测试才能推断。我们进一步将人类表现与同一情境下的一系列大型语言模型进行比较。虽然一些最先进的模型在假设推理准确性上接近人类水平，但它们通常表现出效率较低的探索策略以及类似的合取-析取表现差距。

Original abstract: A long-standing finding in the causal learning literature is that adults struggle to identify conjunctive causal rules, where an effect requires the simultaneous presence of multiple causes, while performing better in disjunctive settings. However, most demonstrations of this ``conjunctive handicap'' rely on passive observation paradigms with limited evidence, where learners have no control over evidence generation. This paper asks whether this bias persists when adults are granted agency through active exploration. Using a modified ``blicket detector'' task, adult participants freely intervened to identify causal objects under conjunctive or disjunctive rule structures. We show that active exploration substantially improves adults' conjunctive causal reasoning, although conjunctive rules still require more tests to infer than disjunctive rules. We further compare human performance to a range of large language models in the same setting. While some state-of-the-art models approach human-level performance on hypothesis inference accuracy, they often exhibit less efficient exploration strategies and similar conjunctive-disjunctive performance gaps.

</details>


### [83] [CAF-Gen: A Multi-Agent System for Enriching Argumentation Structures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06646v2)
*Jakub Bąba,Jarosław A. Chudziak*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出多agent协作框架用于论证结构生成，其迭代创建-审核流程可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: CAF-Gen通过多智能体迭代反馈将浅层论证结构丰富为符合Carneades论证框架的模型，相比单遍生成，提高了数据质量和结构丰富性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前论点挖掘技术捕捉基本主张和前提，但难以处理Carneades论证框架等复杂结构，需要自动化方法对形式论证进行建模。

Method: 提出CAF-Gen框架，采用创建者-审阅者迭代管道，由审阅智能体验证创建智能体的输出以确保结构完整性。

Result: 实验表明，迭代反馈循环改进了数据质量，与原始注释高度一致，并生成结构更丰富的模型。

Conclusion: 多智能体系统能够克服单遍生成的局限性，为自动建模形式论证提供了稳健的方法论。

中文摘要：从自然文本中形式化复杂推理是计算语言学的核心挑战之一。它要求系统不仅理解关键词，还要理解文本中的上下文和复杂推理。当前的论点挖掘（AM）技术能够识别基本主张和前提，但它们往往难以捕捉更丰富的结构信息，这些信息是诸如Carneades论证框架（CAF）等高级模式所需的，该框架包含前提类型、证明标准和论证模式等特征。我们通过引入CAF-Gen来解决这一局限，这是一个自动化的多智能体框架，旨在将浅层论证结构丰富为符合CAF的论证模型。通过采用迭代的创建者-审阅者管道，一个创建者智能体的输出由批判性智能体验证以确保结构完整性。这种多智能体协作对于减轻单遍生成模型典型的结构不稳定至关重要。我们的实验表明，迭代反馈循环提高了所得数据的质量，并与原始注释实现了强对齐，同时产生了结构更丰富的模型。我们的发现表明，多智能体系统可以克服单遍生成的局限，为自动建模形式论证提供了稳健的方法论。

Original abstract: Formalizing complex reasoning from natural text is one of the central challenges in computational linguistics. It requires systems to understand not just keywords but also the context and complex reasoning embedded in a text. Current Argument Mining (AM) techniques identify basic claims and premises, yet they often struggle to capture the richer structural information required by advanced schemas such as the Carneades Argumentation Framework (CAF), which incorporates features such as premise types, proof standards, and argument schemes. We address this limitation by introducing CAF-Gen, an automated multi-agent framework designed to enrich shallow argument structures into CAF-compliant argument models. By employing an iterative Creator-Reviewer pipeline, a creator agent's output is validated by a critical agent to ensure structural integrity. This multi-agent collaboration is crucial for mitigating the structural instability typical of single-pass generative models. Our experiments demonstrate that the iterative feedback loop improves the quality of the resulting data and achieves strong alignment with the original annotations, while producing structurally richer models. Our findings show that the multi-agent system can overcome the limitations of single-pass generation, providing a robust methodology for the automated modeling of formal argumentation.

</details>

### [84] [GenTI: Benchmarking LLMs for Autonomous IDPS Rule Generation for Unseen Attacks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05844v1)
*Hassan Jalil Hadi,Rehana Yasmin,Ali Shoker*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM自动生成IDPS规则，含链式推理与验证，agent应用但偏离代码优化

TL;DR: GenTI是一个LLM驱动的基准，通过大规模标注数据集和LLM流水线自动生成IDPS规则，显著提升未见攻击检测率并降低误报率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有IDPS规则手工编制、适应性差，公共数据集缺乏结构化信息以支持自动规则合成，因此需要一种自动化、自适应的规则生成方法。

Method: 构建GTI数据集（15万+规则，含CTI标注），设计LLM流水线（结构化提示、CoT推理、CoVe验证），生成可部署规则并在Snort/Suricata上实时评估。

Result: 复合规则质量89.4%，CTI覆盖率94.8%，未见攻击检测率从45%提升至87.4%，误报率从8.5%降至2.3%。

Conclusion: GenTI建立了首个规则级CTI与LLM自动化耦合的大规模基准，支持自适应、自我演化的IDPS。

中文摘要：基于规则的入侵检测与防御系统（IDPS）能够提供精确的攻击检测和缓解，但其手工编制的、基于签名的规则限制了其对新兴攻击和零日攻击的适应性。此外，现有的公共数据集（例如CICIDS2017、UNSW-NB15）侧重于流量分类，提供的结构化信息很少，无法支持自动规则合成或防御逻辑。为了解决这一缺口，我们提出了生成式威胁情报（GenTI）——一个用于自动生成针对未见攻击的IDPS规则的LLM驱动基准。该数据集（GTI）汇集了来自Snort、Suricata、Emerging Threats的超过15万条检测和防御规则，以及5万条YARA规则，每条规则都标注了协议行为、有效载荷签名、上下文关系、与网络威胁情报（CTI）的映射，以及可操作的响应类型（告警、丢弃、拒绝）。此外，在此语料库的基础上，我们设计了一个基于LLM的流水线，通过结构化提示工程、思维链（CoT）推理以及用于语法、语义和安全验证的验证链（CoVe）循环，将分析师提示和代表性有效载荷转换为可部署的规则。生成的规则在Snort/Suricata上实时执行，并通过语法准确性、语义相似性、CTI覆盖率、安全有效性以及未见攻击检测进行评估。此外，我们的GenTI实例化实现了89.4%的综合规则质量分数，94.8%的CTI覆盖率，将未见攻击检测率从45%提高到87.4%，并将误报率从8.5%降低到2.3%。总体而言，GenTI建立了第一个将规则级CTI与LLM自动化紧密耦合的大规模基准，支持自适应的、自我演化的IDPS。

Original abstract: Rule-based Intrusion Detection and Prevention Systems (IDPS) offer precise attack detection as well as mitigation, however their manually crafted, signature-driven rules limit adaptability to emerging and zero-day threats. Additionally, existing public datasets (e.g., CICIDS2017, UNSW-NB15) focus on traffic classification and provide little structured information to support automatic rule synthesis or prevention logic. To address this gap, we propose Generative Thread Intelligence (GenTI) \footnote{GenTI refers to the proposed framework, and GTI refers to the dataset.} an LLM-driven benchmark for automatic generation of IDPS rules targeting unseen attacks. The dataset (GTI) aggregates over 150k detection and prevention rules from Snort, Suricata, Emerging Threats, as well as 50k YARA, each annotated with protocol behavior, payload signatures, contextual relationships, mappings to Cyber Threat Intelligence (CTI), along with actionable response types (alert, drop, reject). Moreover, on top of this corpus we design an LLM-based pipeline that transforms analyst prompts and representative payloads into deployable rules via structured prompt engineering, Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning, as well as a Chain-of-Verification (CoVe) loop for syntactic, semantic, and security validation. The generated rules are executed in real time on (Snort/Suricata) and evaluated by syntax accuracy, semantic similarity, CTI coverage, security effectiveness as well as unseen attacks detection. Furthermore, our GenTI instantiation achieves a composite rule-quality score of 89.4\%, with 94.8\% CTI coverage, improving unseen attacks detection from 45\% to 87.4\% and reducing the false-positive rate from 8.5\% to 2.3\%. Overall, GenTI establishes the first large-scale benchmark that tightly couples rule-level CTI with LLM-based automation, enabling adaptive, self-evolving IDPS.

</details>


### [85] [Will the Agent Recuse Itself? Measuring LLM-Agent Compliance with In-Band Access-Deny Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06460v2)
*Thamilvendhan Munirathinam*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出agent合规性信号，对agent安全控制有启发，可迁移至coding agent权限管理

TL;DR: 提出一种类似robots.txt的“回避信号”，让服务器请求LLM代理自愿退出，实验表明代理100%遵守，但信号是合作性的，可被授权覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主LLM代理在没有人类监督的情况下操作基础设施，缺乏标准方式告知代理资源不可访问，现有访问控制要么允许进入要么硬性拒绝，无法实现细粒度的自愿退出机制。

Method: 定义回避信号为开放微型标准，实现三个适配器（SSH横幅/PAM钩子、PostgreSQL协议代理、Kubernetes准入webhook），部署在生产主机上进行受控实验，观察LLM代理（GPT-4o、GPT-4o-mini、Claude Code）在信号存在与不存在时的行为。

Result: 信号存在时代理100%回避，无信号时100%完成任务；且信号是合作性的，操作员授权可使最强模型继续执行，其他模型仍遵守信号。

Conclusion: 回避信号能有效诱导LLM代理自愿退出，但依赖于代理的合作性而非强制性，是一种实用的协同治理机制，适用于当前LLM代理的访问控制场景。

中文摘要：随着自主LLM代理越来越多地持有真实凭证并在无人参与的情况下操作基础设施，操作员没有标准方式告知代理某个资源不可访问。访问控制要么让代理进入（它拥有有效凭证），要么硬性拒绝（与其他客户端无区别）。我们提出了第三种模式：一个轻量级的、发布的带内拒绝信号——回避信号——服务器通过协议的现有信道（SSH横幅、PostgreSQL NOTICE）发出，要求连接的自动化代理自愿退出。这是一种合作治理控制，是robots.txt对于实时访问的类比；它明确不是一个安全边界。其价值完全是经验性的，据我们所知尚未被测量：合规的LLM代理真的会遵守这种信号吗？我们将该信号定义为一个开放的微型标准，实现了三个零或低足迹适配器（SSH横幅/PAM钩子、PostgreSQL线路协议代理和Kubernetes准入webhook），将它们部署在一个生产主机上，并进行了一个受控实验，其中新代理被赋予一个良性操作任务并观察其是否回避。在一个试点中（SSH；OpenAI GPT-4o和GPT-4o-mini；以及Claude Code作为已部署的代理），该信号干净地诱导了回避——当信号存在时100%回避，而无信号控制组中100%完成任务——并且有启示性地表现为合作性而非绝对性信号：一个明确的操作员授权框架使最有能力的模型继续执行，而其他代理则继续遵循主机策略。我们发布了标准、适配器和实验框架以便复现。

Original abstract: As autonomous LLM agents increasingly hold real credentials and operate infrastructure without a human in the loop, operators have no standard way to tell an agent that a resource is off-limits. Access controls either let the agent in (it has valid credentials) or hard-fail it (indistinguishable from any other client). We propose a third mode: a lightweight, published in-band deny signal -- the Recuse Signal -- that a server emits over a protocol's existing channels (an SSH banner, a PostgreSQL NOTICE) asking a connecting automated agent to voluntarily withdraw. This is a cooperative governance control, the robots.txt analogue for live access; it is explicitly not a security boundary. Its value is entirely empirical and, to our knowledge, unmeasured: do compliant LLM agents actually honor such a signal? We define the signal as an open mini-standard, implement three zero- or low-footprint adapters (an SSH banner/PAM hook, a PostgreSQL wire-protocol proxy, and a Kubernetes admission webhook), deploy them on a live production host, and run a controlled experiment in which fresh agents are given a benign operations task and observed for recusal. In a pilot (SSH; OpenAI GPT-4o and GPT-4o-mini; and Claude Code as a deployed agent), the signal cleanly induces recusal -- 100% recusal when present versus 100% task completion in a no-signal control -- and, revealingly, behaves as a cooperative rather than absolute signal: an explicit operator-authorization framing flips the most capable model to proceed, while other agents continue to defer to the on-host policy. We release the standard, adapters, and experiment harness for reproduction.

</details>


### [86] [The Custody Envelope Threshold: Authority-Scaled Admission of External Artifacts in Institutional Infrastructure](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06767v1)
*Amadeus Brandes*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Custody Envelope Threshold模型，用于评估外部工件接纳的防御性，并通过四条件阈值判断机构应采取何种策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外部工件易获取但难治理，直接机构接纳需要满足封闭性条件，否则需要其他策略。

Method: 构建四条件有序工具，结合引用监控、最小权限和交易成本理论，应用于多种工件类型并设计验证实验。

Result: 框架可应用于包依赖、CI/CD、容器镜像等场景，并提供了OSF复制包以供测试。

Conclusion: 高审查机构应针对高权限工件加强托管封闭性，否则需采用代理、中介等替代策略。

中文摘要：现代基础设施依赖于外部维护的工件，例如包注册表依赖项、CI/CD操作、容器镜像、Terraform提供程序和模块、开发者扩展、模型工件以及AI工具服务器。这些工件易于获取，但机构难以接纳、治理和撤销。本文提出了托管信封阈值，这是一种基于权限缩放的工件接纳模型。它认为，只有当对象身份、入口路径和撤销能力相对于委托给工件的执行权限足够封闭时，直接机构接纳才是合理的。当不满足此阈值时，机构倾向于代理、策略中介、供应商中介、内部化、隔离或拒绝该工件。该框架被操作化为一个四条件有序工具，并与引用监控推理、最小权限和交易成本经济学相关联。它应用于包依赖项、GitHub Actions、容器镜像、Terraform提供程序和模块、开发者扩展以及开放模型工件，其中模型上下文协议（MCP）服务器作为保留证据。本文还指定了验证设计、确定性预测函数和OSF复制包，用于测试高审查机构是否会在高权限工件的托管封闭性方面趋同。

Original abstract: Modern infrastructure depends on externally maintained artifacts such as package-registry dependencies, CI/CD actions, container images, Terraform providers and modules, developer extensions, model artifacts, and AI tool servers. These artifacts are easy to fetch but difficult for institutions to admit, govern, and revoke. This paper proposes the Custody Envelope Threshold, an authority-scaled model of artifact admission. It argues that direct institutional admission is defensible only when object identity, ingress path, and revocation capacity are sufficiently closed relative to the execution authority delegated to the artifact. When this threshold is not met, institutions tend to proxy, policy-mediate, vendor-mediate, internalize, quarantine, or reject the artifact. The framework is operationalized as a four-condition ordinal instrument and connected to reference-monitor reasoning, least privilege, and transaction cost economics. It is applied to package dependencies, GitHub Actions, container images, Terraform providers and modules, developer extensions, and open model artifacts, with Model Context Protocol (MCP) servers treated as held-out evidence. The paper also specifies a validation design, deterministic prediction function, and OSF replication package for testing whether high-scrutiny institutions converge toward stronger custody closure for high-authority artifacts.

</details>

### [87] [Data Flow Control: Data Safety Policies for AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05679v1)
*Charlie Summers,Eugene Wu*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: AI agent数据安全策略框架，涉及agent数据流控制，通用安全方法

TL;DR: 提出Data Flow Control框架，通过不物化溯源的查询重写层Passant，在多个DBMS中高效执行数据安全策略，几乎零开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 查询的正确性不等于安全性，需在数据基础设施层面强制执行监管、隐私和业务约束。

Method: 定义基于溯源多项式的聚合谓词作为策略语言，设计可移植查询重写层Passant，在不物化溯源的情况下执行DFC策略。

Result: 在五个DBMS引擎上，Passant实现约0%的开销，性能比替代方案高几个数量级。

Conclusion: Data Flow Control是将数据安全从提示和事后检查转移到数据基础设施的第一步，开源可用。

中文摘要：代理越来越多地代表用户生成SQL、编排管道和自动化数据分析。虽然最近的工作提高了查询的正确性，但正确性并不等于安全性。一个查询在语义上可能有效，但违反了管理数据如何组合和发布的监管、隐私或业务约束。我们认为，执行这些约束从根本上说是一个数据基础设施问题。本文介绍了数据流控制（DFC），一个在DBMS查询内声明式指定和保证对元组级数据流进行策略执行的框架。一个关键挑战是定义一种策略语言，该语言对优化器不变，但能高效地大规模执行。我们将数据安全形式化为关于溯源多项式的聚合谓词，并提出了Passant，一个可移植的查询重写层，它在不物化溯源的情况下执行DFC策略。在五个DBMS引擎——DuckDB、Umbra、PostgreSQL、DataFusion和SQLServer上，Passant实现了约0%的开销，并且性能比替代方案高出几个数量级。因此，数据流控制是将数据安全从提示和事后检查转移到数据基础设施的第一步。数据流控制开源可在https://github.com/dataflowcontrol/data-flow-control获取。

Original abstract: Agents increasingly generate SQL, orchestrate pipelines, and automate data analysis on behalf of users. While recent work improves query correctness, correctness is not safety. A query may be semantically valid yet violate regulatory, privacy, or business constraints that govern how data may be combined and released. We argue that enforcing such constraints is fundamentally a data infrastructure problem.
  This paper introduces Data Flow Control (DFC), a framework to declaratively specify and guarantee policy enforcement over tuple-level data flows within a DBMS query. A key challenge is defining a policy language that is optimizer-invariant yet efficient to enforce at scale. We formalize data safety as aggregate predicates over provenance monomials and present Passant, a portable query rewriting layer that enforces DFC policies without materializing provenance. Across five DBMS engines -- DuckDB, Umbra, PostgreSQL, DataFusion, and SQLServer -- Passant achieves ~0% overhead and outperforms alternatives by orders of magnitude. As a result, Data Flow Control is the first step towards moving data safety from prompts and post-hoc checks into the data infrastructure. Data Flow Control is available open source at https://github.com/dataflowcontrol/data-flow-control.

</details>


### [88] [TOKI: A Bitemporal Operator Algebra for Contradiction Resolution in LLM-Agent Persistent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06240v1)
*Ziming Wang*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 提出位时算子解决LLM agent持久记忆中的矛盾，涉及agent记忆管理方法。

TL;DR: 本文揭示了LLM代理持久内存中矛盾解决本质上是写入时并发控制，提出了TOKI框架，通过类型化时态操作符和审计行机制，正式定义了隔离、模式和溯源之间的契约，并证明了其健全性，避免了现有系统中的写入时异常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生产系统使用多种矛盾解决启发式，但未声明其隔离级别或允许的写入时异常，导致契约缺失，可能引发数据一致性问题。

Method: 将四种矛盾解决启发式类型化为基于双行模式的时态操作符家族，每个操作符附带隔离前提和溯源注释；通过四个健全性定理形式化契约，并扩展到操作符流水线和n元冲突集；利用关系调度模型证明键控日志对重放一致性的必要性，并构建判决矩阵对比八个系统。

Result: TOKI在保留语言模型判断器的同时排除了三种写入时异常，而其他基线至少允许一种；审计行防御在LoCoMo自然工作负载上提升0.86，消除类型化内存层导致准确度下降0.49；跨系统比较未声称优越性。

Conclusion: 贡献在于正式定义了写入时正确性契约，跨隔离、模式和溯源证明其健全性，明确了生产系统隐含但未明确的保证，并提供了可实现的TOKI框架。

中文摘要：持久内存对于LLM代理来说是写密集型的底层：每个信念更新都是版本化写入，新声明可能与存储的声明矛盾。生产系统使用四种解决启发式（最后写入者获胜、基于证据的合并、等待确认、按规则策略），但没有一个声明其假设的隔离级别或允许的写入时异常。我们表明矛盾解决是写入时并发控制，并明确缺失的契约。TOKI将四种启发式类型化为基于双行模式的时态操作符家族，每个操作符都有隔离前提和保留失败事实在审计行中的溯源注释。四个健全性定理闭合了隔离、模式和溯源之间的契约，将保证提升到操作符流水线，并将折叠操作符扩展到n元冲突集。一个紧致性证明表明，在关系调度模型内，裁决判断器的键控日志对于重放一致性是必要的，而每个审计基线都省略了这一点。八个系统的判决矩阵定位了差距：每个在写入路径上保留语言模型判断器的基线至少允许三种写入时异常之一（重放不一致、信念漂移偏斜、审计擦除）；基于内容寻址的引擎层比较器仅通过移除判断器来避免它们，而TOKI独自在保留判断器的同时排除所有三种。在其一个自然工作负载切片上，审计行防御使LoCoMo移动0.86，而消除类型化内存层在1444个可回答的LoCoMo问题上移除0.49准确度；跨系统比较仍能力不足，未声称优越性。贡献在于契约：一个写入时正确性规范，跨隔离、模式和溯源证明健全，明确了每个生产启发式假设但没有部署系统明确的保证。

Original abstract: Persistent memory for an LLM agent is a write-heavy substrate: every belief update is a versioned write, and a new claim may contradict a stored one. Production systems use four resolution heuristics (last-writer-wins, evidence-weighted merge, await-confirmation, per-rule policy), yet none declares the isolation level it assumes or the write-time anomalies it admits. We show that contradiction resolution is write-time concurrency control and make the missing contract explicit. TOKI types the four heuristics as one family of bitemporal operators over a dual-row schema, each with an isolation precondition and a provenance annotation that preserves the losing fact in an audit row. Four soundness theorems close the contract across isolation, schema, and provenance, lift the guarantees to operator pipelines, and extend the fold operators to n-ary conflict sets. A tightness companion proves that, within the relational schedule model, keyed logging of the adjudicating judge is necessary for replay consistency, which every audited baseline omits. A verdict matrix over eight systems localizes the gap: every baseline that keeps a language-model judge on the write path admits at least one of three write-time anomalies (replay inconsistency, belief-drift skew, audit erasure); a content-addressed engine-layer comparator avoids them only by removing the judge, and TOKI alone excludes all three while keeping it. On its one natural-workload slice the audit-row defence moves LoCoMo by 0.86, and ablating the typed memory layer removes 0.49 accuracy on 1,444 answerable LoCoMo questions; the cross-system comparison stays underpowered and claims no superiority. The contribution is the contract: a write-time correctness specification, proved sound across isolation, schema, and provenance, pinning the guarantee every production heuristic assumes but no deployed system makes explicit.

</details>

# cs.PL [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [AgentCompile: An LLM-Guided Compiler for Direct CUDA Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07665v1)
*Xuanzhe Li,Ziyan Weng,Zhiyu Zhu,Junhui Hou*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: LLM引导的CUDA推理编译器，直接进行自动代码性能优化

TL;DR: AgentCompile利用LLM提供搜索元数据，编译器通过模板生成、验证和选择CUDA实现，在多个Transformer模型上实现4-5倍推理加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer推理需要语义决策来选择优化区域和CUDA实现，现有方法依赖人工或低效搜索，缺乏自动化引导。

Method: LLM基于编译器区域摘要提出语义标签和候选优先级等元数据；编译器通过模板实例化CUDA候选，检查接口和硬件约束，通过经验验证选择延迟最优的实现，并支持回退。

Result: 在Qwen3-1.7B、Qwen3-4B和Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct上，端到端自回归生成平均加速比分别达到5.66x、4.05x和4.26x。

Conclusion: AgentCompile有效结合LLM的语义理解与编译器的自动验证和选择，显著提升CUDA推理性能，项目将开源。

中文摘要：Transformer推理越来越依赖专门的编译器和运行时支持，但实际模型图仍然需要语义决策，即哪些区域值得专门优化以及哪些CUDA实现系列是可行的。我们提出了AgentCompile，一个LLM引导的CUDA推理编译器，它仅将LLM输出作为咨询性搜索元数据。给定编译器派生的区域摘要和有界候选空间，LLM提出语义标签、候选优先级、参数提示和风险注释；编译器通过模板实例化CUDA候选，检查接口和硬件约束，经验验证候选，根据测量延迟选择实现，并在不支持或无利可图的专门化时回退。在端到端自回归生成中，AgentCompile在五个代表性工作负载上，相对于PyTorch eager，在Qwen3-1.7B、Qwen3-4B和Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct上分别实现了平均5.66倍、4.05倍和4.26倍的加速。我们将开源该项目。

Original abstract: Transformer inference increasingly depends on specialized compiler and runtime support, but real model graphs still require semantic decisions about which regions are worth specializing and which CUDA implementation families are plausible. We present AgentCompile, an LLM-guided CUDA inference compiler that uses LLM outputs only as advisory search metadata. Given compiler-derived region summaries and bounded candidate spaces, the LLM proposes semantic labels, candidate priorities, parameter hints, and risk annotations; the compiler materializes CUDA candidates through templates, checks interface and hardware constraints, validates candidates empirically, selects implementations by measured latency, and falls back when specialization is unsupported or unprofitable. In end-to-end autoregressive generation, AgentCompile averages 5.66x, 4.05x, and 4.26x speedup over PyTorch eager on Qwen3-1.7B, Qwen3-4B, and Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct, respectively, across five representative workloads. We will open-source the project.

</details>


<div id='econ.EM'></div>

# econ.EM [[Back]](#toc)

### [90] [Econstellar: An Open-Source AI-Augmented Research Engine for Computational Financial Econometrics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05705v1)
*Avishek Bhandari*

Main category: econ.EM

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Econstellar是一个开放源代码的科研引擎，允许用户通过网络浏览器重现和验证金融计量经济学分析，从而缩短研究结果与独立验证之间的距离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决实证研究成本高昂且结果难以被他人复现和验证的问题，缩短研究主张到独立验证的时间。

Method: 采用三个设计选择：将计算放在适合的处理器上、AI助手仅选择解释但不产生数字、使用与已发表研究相同的代码；提供十七种计量经济学方法，价格视为非平稳，所有方法应用于收益率。

Result: 系统已免费开源发布，包含三个软件版本和三个预印本，能够实时重现金融传染研究的标题结果。

Conclusion: 该系统有效缩短了研究主张与独立验证之间的距离，提高了实证研究的透明性和可复现性。

中文摘要：将一个有前景的经济学想法转化为可信的实证发现，在实践中是一项昂贵的任务：它需要大量的专门计算，并且结果很少以他人可以检查或在此基础上构建的形式发布。Econstellar是我们的回应。它是一个开放、公共服务的科研引擎，可以在普通网络浏览器中运行出版级别的金融计量经济学，并解释结果的含义，从而让读者不仅阅读发现，还能重新运行它、改变其输入，并精确追溯其产生过程。三个选择赋予了该系统特色。繁重的计算被放置在适合它的处理器上，而不是被迫用于与任务不匹配的硬件上，这是此类分析很少向公众提供服务的主要原因之一。一个人工智能助手选择和解释分析，但从不产生数字，因此它报告的每个数量都是读者可以复现的真实计算。访问者使用的引擎与生成我们已发表研究中的图表的是同一代码。我们展示了十七种计量经济学方法，每种方法都报告了经过验证的实时值，并可在公共端点上重现，这些计算遵循单一规则：价格被视为非平稳的，所有方法均应用于收益率。该系统还按需从生成它的软件包中重现一项关于金融传染的附带研究的主要结果。该平台是一个活跃研究项目的核心，跨越三个软件版本和三个预印本，现在可以在一个实时公共地址上免费开源使用。我们的目标很简单：缩短研究主张与其他人能够独立验证它之间的时间。

Original abstract: Turning a promising economic idea into a credible empirical finding is, in practice, an expensive undertaking: it demands a great deal of specialised computation, and the results are seldom released in a form that others can check or build upon. Econstellar is our response. It is an open, publicly served research engine that runs publication-grade financial econometrics from an ordinary web browser and explains what the results mean, so that a reader does not merely read a finding but can re-run it, vary its inputs, and trace exactly how it was produced. Three choices give the system its character. The heavy computation is placed on the processor that suits it, rather than forced onto hardware ill-matched to the task, which is much of the reason analysis of this kind is so rarely served to the public. An artificial-intelligence assistant selects and interprets the analyses but never originates a number, so every quantity it reports is a real computation the reader can reproduce. And the engine a visitor exercises is the same code that produced the figures in our published research. We expose seventeen econometric methods, each reported with a verified live value and reproducible at the public endpoint, computed under a single discipline: prices are treated as non-stationary and all methods are applied to returns. The system also regenerates, on demand, the headline result of an accompanying study of financial contagion, from the package that generated it. The platform is the working core of an active research programme spanning three software releases and three preprints, and it is available now, free and open-source, at a live public address. Our aim is a simple one: to shorten the distance between a research claim and the moment another person can independently verify it.

</details>

### [91] [A Finite Certificate for the Positive $n=9$ Vasc Inequality](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06136v1)
*Dakai Guo,Ruichen Qiu,Yichuan Cao,Ruyong Feng*

Main category: cs.SC

Selection reason: AI agent辅助数学证明，展示agent工具使用与验证流程，对通用agent方法有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 在人类引导下，AI智能体MechMath Agent Team证明了Vasc循环不等式的n=9情况，生成了一个覆盖所有40320个排序锥的证书，包含数万叶子节点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明Vasc循环不等式在n=9时的正实数情况，这是一个具有挑战性的数学问题。

Method: 人类引导AI智能体，将有理不等式简化为齐次多项式不等式，通过固定循环最大值和累积间隙参数化排序锥，并生成覆盖所有8!个排序锥的证书。

Result: 成功生成证书，包含36815个系数叶子、2236个Polya乘子叶子和1269个AM-GM中点覆盖叶子，验证了不等式。

Conclusion: AI智能体在人类引导下可以辅助证明复杂的数学不等式，所提方法有效且可审计。

中文摘要：我们证明了Vasc循环不等式的正实数$n=9$情况。该证明是在AI智能体MechMath Agent Team的人类引导辅助下获得的：人类可读部分将有理不等式简化为齐次多项式不等式，固定一个循环最大值，并通过累积间隙对每个排序的固定最大值锥进行参数化；有限部分是一个覆盖所有$8!=40320$个排序锥的证书。MechMath Agent Team通过Python工具调用生成了证书验证工作流程，包括情况拆分、验证程序和终端分类。已发布的证书包含$36815$个系数叶子节点、$2236$个普通Polya乘子叶子节点和$1269$个AM-GM中点覆盖叶子节点。人类作者审核了数学简化与验证逻辑，一个独立制品包含该证书、一个独立验证器以及一个从源码重建的路径。

Original abstract: We prove the positive-real $n=9$ case of the Vasc cyclic inequality. The proof was obtained with human-guided assistance from the AI agent MechMath Agent Team: the human-readable part reduces the rational inequality to a homogeneous polynomial inequality, fixes a cyclic maximum, and parametrizes each sorted fixed-maximum cone by cumulative gaps; the finite part is a certificate covering all $8!=40320$ sorted cones. MechMath Agent Team generated the certificate verification workflow through Python tool calls, including the case split, verification programs, and terminal classifications. The published certificate has $36815$ coefficient leaves, $2236$ ordinary Polya multiplier leaves, and $1269$ AM-GM midpoint overlay leaves. Human authors audited the mathematical reductions and verification logic, and a separate artifact contains the certificate, an independent verifier, and a from-source rebuild route.

</details>

# eess.SY [[Back]](#toc)

### [92] [Development of a Structured Approach for Establishing Mission Engineering Requirements](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05651v1)
*Taylor C. Fazzini,Daniel R. Herber*

Main category: eess.SY

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种在无客户需求时定义任务效能的结构化方法，分解任务意图并引入复杂性因子，支持需求推导和架构集成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统需求工程依赖客户输入，但在客户需求缺失或演变时存在空白，尤其是快速开发项目需要适应性方法。

Method: 分解任务意图，进行可行性评估，使用最佳-最差标度法优先级排序，引入任务复杂性因子，并支持UAF和SysML集成。

Result: 提供了可追溯的Tier 1和2需求推导基础，并通过近距离空中支援示例演示。

Conclusion: 该方法填补了无客户需求时定义任务效能的空白，且支持未来架构框架集成。

中文摘要：本文探讨了这样一个问题：在没有客户需求的情况下，如何系统地定义或近似任务效能？传统的需求工程框架假定有客户输入来定义规格说明，但当利益相关者输入不明确或缺失时，该过程存在空白。快速构建和开发项目（如军事采购、太空资产、基础设施项目等）通常在提案过程中需求和目标会不断演变，因此需要一种更具适应性的方法。为填补这一空白，本文提出了一种结构化方法，将任务意图分解为任务背景、功能、约束、关键维度、效能属性和架构备选方案。该方法进行任务可行性评估，使用最佳-最差标度法对任务关键维度进行优先级排序，并引入任务复杂性因子来定量理解外部任务困难、技术成熟度、证据和信心标准以及任务效用的影响。最终的方法为推导一级和二级需求提供了可追溯的基础。该方法的构建旨在支持未来与统一架构框架（UAF）和系统建模语言（SysML）工件的集成。本文通过一个假设的近距离空中支援任务示例演示了所提出的框架。

Original abstract: This paper addresses the question: How can mission effectiveness be systematically defined or approximated in the absence of customer requirements? Legacy requirements engineering frameworks presuppose customer input to define specifications but leave a gap in the process when stakeholder input is ill-defined or missing. Rapid build and development programs (such as military acquisition, space assets, infrastructure projects, etc.) often see requirement and objective evolutions throughout the proposal process, so a more adaptive method is needed. To address this gap, a structured approach is proposed that decomposes mission intent into mission context, functions, constraints, critical dimensions, effectiveness attributes, and architecture alternatives. This method conducts a mission feasibility assessment, prioritizes mission-critical dimensions using Best-Worst Scaling, and introduces a mission complexity factor to quantitatively understand the impacts of external mission difficulties, technology maturity, evidence and confidence standards, and mission utility. The resulting method provides a traceable basis for deriving Tier 1 and 2 requirements. The approach is structured to support future Unified Architecture Framework (UAF) and Systems Modeling Language (SysML) artifact integration. The proposed framework is demonstrated using a notional close air support mission example.

</details>
